 216:   function escapeHtml(value) {
 217:     return String(value ?? "")
 218:       .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
 219:       .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
 220:       .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
 221:       .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
 222:       .replace(/'/g, "&#39;");
 223:   }
 224: 
 225:   function formatDateTime(isoString) {
 226:     try {
 227:       return new Date(isoString).toLocaleString();
 228:     } catch {
 229:       return String(isoString || "");
 230:     }
 231:   }
 232: 
 233:   function makeReportId(prefix = "SL-REPORT") {
 234:     const stamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[-:TZ.]/g, "").slice(0, 14);
 235:     return `${prefix}-${stamp}`;
 236:   }

 247:   function setExportEnabled(enabled) {
 248:     if (els.exportReport) els.exportReport.disabled = !enabled;
 249:     if (els.saveSnapshot) els.saveSnapshot.disabled = !enabled;
 250:     if (window.ScopedLabsExport) {
 251:       if (enabled && typeof window.ScopedLabsExport.refresh === "function") {
 252:         window.ScopedLabsExport.refresh();
 253:       } else if (!enabled && typeof window.ScopedLabsExport.invalidate === "function") {
 254:         window.ScopedLabsExport.invalidate("Inputs changed. Run the calculator again to refresh export.");
 255:       }
 256:     }
 257:   }

 263:   function updateExportControls(message) {
 264:     const unlocked = hasExportAccess();
 265:     const ready = !!currentReport;
 266: 
 267:     setExportEnabled(unlocked && ready);
 268: 
 269:     if (message !== undefined) {
 270:       setExportStatus(message);

 272:     }

 275:       setExportStatus("Export is available with Access Control category unlock.");

 278:

 281:       return;
 282:     }
 283:

 285:   }

 379:             ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.14)";

 405:         afterDatasetsDraw(chartInstance) {

 411:           const { top, bottom } = chartArea;

 413:           ctx.save();
 414: 
 415:           const rx = x.getPixelForValue(recommendedLimit);

1146:       insight:

1389:   function calc() {
1390:     const roles = num(els.roles.value);
1391:     const areas = num(els.areas.value);
1392:     const schedules = num(els.schedules.value);
1393:     const groups = num(els.doorGroups.value);
1394:     const complexity = els.complexity.value;
1395: 
1396:     if (roles <= 0 || areas <= 0 || schedules < 0 || groups < 0) {
1397:       invalidate("Enter valid positive values, then run analysis.");
1398:       return;
1399:     }
1400: 
1401:     const base = roles * areas;
1402:     const complexityFactor = getComplexityFactor(complexity);
1403:     const schedulePenalty = 1 + schedules * 0.1;
1404:     const groupPenalty = 1 + groups * 0.05;
1405: 
1406:     const total = Math.round(base * schedulePenalty * groupPenalty * complexityFactor);
1407:     const combinations = base;
1408:     const scalingPressure = total / Math.max(1, roles + areas);
1409:     const recommendedLimit = getRecommendedLimit(complexity);
1410:     const overshoot = Math.max(0, total - recommendedLimit);
1411:     const adminLoadIndex = Number(((schedules * 0.8) + (groups * 0.6) + (roles * 0.4)).toFixed(1));
1412: 
1413:     const risk = getRisk(total);
1414: 
1415:     let thresholdMessage = "Structure remains below the recommended complexity limit.";
1416: 
1417:     if (total > recommendedLimit) {
1418:       thresholdMessage = `Design exceeds the recommended complexity limit by ${overshoot} levels.`;
1419:     } else {
1420:       thresholdMessage = `Design remains ${recommendedLimit - total} levels under the recommended limit.`;
1421:     }
1422: 
1423:     els.results.innerHTML = [
1424:       row("Access Levels", total),
1425:       row("Role-Area Combinations", combinations),
1426:       row("Scaling Pressure", scalingPressure.toFixed(1)),
1427:       row("Admin Load Index", adminLoadIndex.toFixed(1)),
1428:       row("Recommended Limit", recommendedLimit),
1429:       row("Complexity", risk.label),
1430:       row("Threshold Check", thresholdMessage),
1431:       row("Engineering Insight", risk.insight)
1432:     ].join("");
1433: 
1434:     renderChart(total, roles, areas, schedules, groups, recommendedLimit);
1435: 
1436:     ScopedLabsAnalyzer.clearAnalysisBlock(els.analysis);
1437:     ScopedLabsAnalyzer.showContinue(els.continueWrap, els.continueBtn);
1438: 
1439:     if (els.completeWrap) els.completeWrap.style.display = "block";
1440: 
1441:     const flowData = {
1442:       total,
1443:       risk: risk.label,
1444:       combinations,
1445:       scalingPressure,
1446:       adminLoadIndex,
1447:       recommendedLimit,
1448:       overshoot
1449:     };
1450: 
1451:     ScopedLabsAnalyzer.writeFlow(FLOW_KEYS[STEP], {
1452:       category: CATEGORY,
1453:       step: STEP,
1454:       lane: LANE,
1455:       data: flowData
1456:     });
1457: 
1458:     currentReport = buildReportPayload({
1459:       status: risk.status,
1460:       summary: risk.summary,
1461:       interpretation: risk.insight,
1462:       inputs: {
1463:         roles,
1464:         areas,
1465:         schedules,
1466:         doorGroups: groups,
1467:         complexityLabel: complexity.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + complexity.slice(1)
1468:       },
1469:       outputs: {
1470:         total,
1471:         combinations,
1472:         scalingPressure,
1473:         adminLoadIndex,
1474:         recommendedLimit,
1475:         riskLabel: risk.label,
1476:         thresholdMessage,
1477:         overshoot
1478:       }
1479:     });
1480: 
1481:     updateExportControls();
1482:   }

1485:     els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);

1487:

1007:   function getStrategyFactor(strategy) {
1008:     if (strategy === "minimal") return 0.65;
1009:     if (strategy === "balanced") return 1.0;
1010:     return 1.35;
1011:   }
1012: 
1013:   function getTypeFactor(type) {
1014:     return type === "hard" ? 1.25 : 0.75;
1015:   }
1016: 
1017:   function getRecommendedZones(entrances, interior, floors, strategy) {
1018:     let perimeterZones = 2;
1019:     let interiorZones = 0;
1020:     let floorZones = 0;
1021: 
1022:     if (strategy === "minimal") {
1023:       perimeterZones = 2;
1024:       interiorZones = Math.round(interior * 0.15);
1025:       floorZones = 0;
1026:     } else if (strategy === "balanced") {
1027:       perimeterZones = 2;
1028:       interiorZones = Math.round(interior * 0.6);
1029:       floorZones = floors > 1 ? Math.round((floors - 1) * 0.5) : 0;
1030:     } else {
1031:       perimeterZones = 2;
1032:       interiorZones = interior;
1033:       floorZones = Math.max(0, floors - 1);
1034:     }
1035: 
1036:     const total = Math.max(2, perimeterZones + interiorZones + floorZones);
1037: 
1038:     return {
1039:       total,
1040:       perimeterZones,
1041:       interiorZones,
1042:       floorZones
1043:     };
1044:   }
1045: 
1046:   function getOperationalRisk(complexityIndex, type, strategy) {
1047:     if (type === "hard" && (strategy === "strict" || complexityIndex >= 14)) {
1048:       return "HIGH";
1049:     }
1050: 
1051:     if (complexityIndex >= 9) {
1052:       return "MODERATE";
1053:     }
1054: 
1055:     return "LOW";
1056:   }
1057: 
1058:   function getModeRecommendation(type, strategy, complexityIndex) {
1059:     if (type === "hard" && complexityIndex >= 12) {
1060:       return "Consider SOFT APB or narrower enforcement scope";
1061:     }
1062: 
1063:     if (strategy === "minimal") {
1064:       return "Perimeter-focused APB is likely enough";
1065:     }
1066: 
1067:     if (strategy === "balanced") {
1068:       return "Balanced APB with key interior checkpoints is appropriate";
1069:     }
1070: 
1071:     return "Strict APB only makes sense if operations can tolerate enforcement friction";
1072:   }
1073: 
1074:   function getInterpretation({
1075:     zones,
1076:     pairedEntrances,
1077:     operationalRisk
1078:   }) {
1079:     if (operationalRisk === "HIGH") {
1080:       return `This anti-passback design is enforcement-heavy. With ${zones} recommended zones and ${pairedEntrances} paired perimeter transitions, hard APB can easily create nuisance lockouts if reads are missed or circulation paths are inconsistent. Keep APB scope tighter unless you have a strong threat model and reliable bidirectional read coverage.`;
1081:     }
1082: 
1083:     if (operationalRisk === "MODERATE") {
1084:       return "This design is workable, but it needs discipline. The zone count and transition structure are high enough that operator training, exception handling, and reader placement quality will determine whether APB improves control or just adds friction.";
1085:     }
1086: 
1087:     return "This anti-passback design stays relatively manageable. The recommended zone structure is restrained enough that APB can add useful control without becoming an administrative burden, especially if exemptions and emergency paths are planned cleanly.";
1088:   }

1297:         scales: {
1298:           x: {
1299:             beginAtZero: true,
1300:             suggestedMax: chartMax,
1301:             ticks: {
1302:               color: "rgba(220, 238, 230, 0.78)"
1303:             },
1304:             grid: {
1305:               color: "rgba(110, 160, 140, 0.10)"
1306:             },
1307:             title: {
1308:               display: true,
1309:               text: "Operational Magnitude",
1310:               color: "rgba(230, 255, 240, 0.92)"
1311:             }
1312:           },
1313:           y: {
1314:             ticks: {
1315:               color: "rgba(228, 245, 235, 0.92)"
1316:             },
1317:             grid: {
1318:               display: false
1319:             }
1320:           }
1321:         }
1322:       },
1323:       plugins: [chartBgPlugin, thresholdBandPlugin]
1324:     });
1325: 
1326:     els.chart.style.width = "100%";
1327:     els.chart.style.height = "340px";
1328: 
1329:     if (els.chart.parentElement) {
1330:       els.chart.parentElement.style.minHeight = "340px";
1331:     }
1332:   }
1333: 
1334:   function calc() {
1335:     const entrances = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("entrances")));
1336:     const interior = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("interiorAreas")));
1337:     const floors = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n("floors")));
1338:     const strategy = els.strategy.value;
1339:     const type = els.type.value;
1340: 
1341:     const zoneBreakdown = getRecommendedZones(entrances, interior, floors, strategy);
1342:     const pairedFactor = type === "hard" ? 1.0 : 0.6;
1343:     const pairedEntrances = Math.round(entrances * pairedFactor);
1344: 
1345:     const complexityIndexRaw =
1346:       (zoneBreakdown.total * getStrategyFactor(strategy) * 0.9) +
1347:       (pairedEntrances * 0.45) +
1348:       ((floors - 1) * 0.8) +
1349:       (interior * 0.25) +
1350:       (getTypeFactor(type) * 1.2);
1351: 
1352:     const complexityIndex = Number(clamp(complexityIndexRaw, 1, 18).toFixed(1));
1353: 
1354:     const enforcementExposure = Number(
1355:       clamp((pairedEntrances * getTypeFactor(type)) + (zoneBreakdown.total * 0.35), 1, 18).toFixed(1)
1356:     );
1357: 
1358:     const operationalRisk = getOperationalRisk(complexityIndex, type, strategy);
1359:     const modeRecommendation = getModeRecommendation(type, strategy, complexityIndex);
1360: 
1361:     let recommendedType = type.toUpperCase();
1362: 
1363:     if (type === "hard" && operationalRisk === "HIGH") {
1364:       recommendedType = "SOFT or SELECTIVE HARD";
1365:     } else if (type === "soft" && strategy === "minimal") {
1366:       recommendedType = "SOFT";
1367:     }
1368: 
1369:     const interpretation = getInterpretation({
1370:       zones: zoneBreakdown.total,
1371:       pairedEntrances,
1372:       operationalRisk
1373:     });
1374: 
1375:     render([
1376:       row("Recommended Zones", zoneBreakdown.total),
1377:       row("Perimeter Zones", zoneBreakdown.perimeterZones),
1378:       row("Interior Zones", zoneBreakdown.interiorZones),
1379:       row("Floor Segments", zoneBreakdown.floorZones),
1380:       row("Suggested Paired Entrances (IN/OUT)", pairedEntrances),
1381:       row("APB Complexity Index", complexityIndex),
1382:       row("Operational Risk", operationalRisk),
1383:       row("Recommended Enforcement Mode", recommendedType),
1384:       row("Design Guidance", modeRecommendation),
1385:       row("Engineering Interpretation", interpretation)
1386:     ]);
1387: 
1388:     lastMetrics = {
1389:       recommendedZones: zoneBreakdown.total,
1390:       pairedEntrances,
1391:       complexityIndex,
1392:       enforcementExposure
1393:     };
1394: 
1395:     renderChart(lastMetrics);
1396: 
1397:     currentReport = buildCurrentReportPayload();
1398:     updateExportControls();
1399:   }
1400: 
1401:   function resetResults(message = "Enter values and press Calculate.") {
1402:     if (els.results) {
1403:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>`;
1404:     }
1405: 
1406:     destroyChart();
1407:     lastMetrics = null;
1408:     currentReport = null;
1409:     updateExportControls();
1410:   }
1411: 
1412:   function invalidate() {
1413:     resetResults("Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results.");
1414:   }
1415: 
1416:   function reset() {
1417:     if (els.entrances) els.entrances.value = 6;
1418:     if (els.interiorAreas) els.interiorAreas.value = 4;
1419:     if (els.floors) els.floors.value = 2;
1420:     if (els.strategy) els.strategy.value = "minimal";
1421:     if (els.type) els.type.value = "soft";
1422: 
1423:     resetResults("Enter values and press Calculate.");
1424:   }
1425: 
1426:   if (els.calc) {
1427:     els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);
1428:   }
1429: 
1430:   if (els.reset) {
1431:     els.reset.addEventListener("click", reset);
1432:   }
1433: 
1434:   [
1435:     els.entrances,
1436:     els.interiorAreas,
1437:     els.floors,
1438:     els.strategy,
1439:     els.type
1440:   ].forEach((el) => {
1441:     if (!el) return;
1442:     el.addEventListener("input", invalidate);
1443:     el.addEventListener("change", invalidate);
1444:   });
1445: 
1446:   [
1447:     els.reportTitle,
1448:     els.projectName,
1449:     els.clientName,
1450:     els.preparedBy,
1451:     els.customNotes
1452:   ].forEach((el) => {
1453:     if (!el) return;
1454:     el.addEventListener("input", () => {
1455:       if (!currentReport) return;
1456:       updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
1457:     });
1458:   });
1459: 
1460:   if (els.chart) {
1461:     els.chart.style.width = "100%";
1462:     els.chart.style.height = "340px";
1463: 
1464:     if (els.chart.parentElement) {
1465:       els.chart.parentElement.style.minHeight = "340px";
1466:     }
1467:   }
1468: 
1469:   resetResults();
1470: })();

 186:   function readSnapshots(key) {
 187:     try {
 188:       const raw = localStorage.getItem(key);
 189:       const parsed = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : [];
 190:       return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
 191:     } catch {
 192:       return [];
 193:     }
 194:   }
 195: 
 196:   function writeSnapshots(key, items) {
 197:     localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items));
 198:   }
 199: 
 200:   function saveSnapshot(key, payload, limit = 25) {
 201:     const existing = readSnapshots(key);
 202:     existing.unshift({
 203:       ...payload,
 204:       savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
 205:     });
 206: 
 207:     const trimmed = existing.slice(0, limit);
 208:     writeSnapshots(key, trimmed);
 209:     return trimmed.length;
 210:   }

 562:   function openReportWindow(payload) {
 563:     try {
 564:       const html = buildReportHTML(payload);
 565:       const blob = new Blob([html], { type: "text/html" });
 566:       const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
 567:       const win = window.open(url, "_blank");
 568: 
 569:       if (!win) return false;
 570: 
 571:       setTimeout(() => {
 572:         URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
 573:       }, 10000);
 574: 
 575:       return true;
 576:     } catch (err) {
 577:       console.error("Export report open failed:", err);
 578:       return false;
 579:     }
 580:   }

 582:   function classifyUtilization(utilization) {
 583:     if (utilization < 10) {
 584:       return {
 585:         fit: "Excellent headroom",
 586:         status: "HEALTHY",
 587:         summary:
 588:           "The selected credential format has abundant numbering headroom for the expected badge population.",
 589:         interpretation:
 590:           "This format leaves abundant numbering headroom relative to the expected badge population. Collision pressure is low, and future migration pressure should remain manageable if badge count grows modestly."
 591:       };
 592:     }
 593: 
 594:     if (utilization < 30) {
 595:       return {
 596:         fit: "Good headroom",
 597:         status: "HEALTHY",
 598:         summary:
 599:           "The selected credential format has comfortable remaining capacity for the expected badge population.",
 600:         interpretation:
 601:           "This format still has comfortable remaining capacity. The design should scale reasonably well, although format standardization and clean documentation still matter if multiple sites, tenants, or credential batches are involved."
 602:       };
 603:     }
 604: 
 605:     if (utilization < 60) {
 606:       return {
 607:         fit: "Moderate headroom",
 608:         status: "WATCH",
 609:         summary:
 610:           "The selected credential format is workable, but remaining numbering headroom is no longer generous.",
 611:         interpretation:
 612:           "This format is workable, but headroom is no longer generous. Growth, tenant separation, replacement badge ranges, or mixed credential populations can consume the remaining numbering space faster than expected."
 613:       };
 614:     }
 615: 
 616:     if (utilization < 90) {
 617:       return {
 618:         fit: "Tight / risk of collisions",
 619:         status: "WATCH",
 620:         summary:
 621:           "The selected credential format is entering a tight planning band and should be reviewed before broader rollout.",
 622:         interpretation:
 623:           "This format is entering a tight planning band. You may still deploy it, but future growth and migration flexibility are becoming constrained enough that collisions, numbering overlap, or format partitioning deserve attention now."
 624:       };
 625:     }
 626: 
 627:     return {
 628:       fit: "Over capacity / collision likely",
 629:       status: "RISK",
 630:       summary:
 631:         "The selected credential format is effectively overcommitted for the expected badge population.",
 632:       interpretation:
 633:         "This format is effectively overcommitted for the expected badge population. Collision risk or numbering overlap becomes likely enough that a larger or more carefully partitioned format should be considered before rollout."
 634:     };
 635:   }
 636: 
 637:   function buildBestPractices() {
 638:     return [
 639:       "Standardize one format across the site to avoid reader/panel interpretation mismatches.",
 640:       "Document the exact format clearly: bit length, facility code range, and card range.",
 641:       "If multi-tenant, partition facility codes intentionally instead of ad hoc growth.",
 642:       "If migrating, plan card translation or dual-format acceptance during the cutover window."
 643:     ].join(" ");
 644:   }
 645: 
 646:   function calc() {
 647:     const fcDigits = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("fcDigits")));
 648:     const cardDigits = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n("cardDigits")));
 649:     const fmt = els.fmt?.value || "decimal";
 650:     const bits = parseInt(els.bits?.value || "26", 10);
 651:     const population = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("pop")));
 652: 
 653:     const fcCap = pow10(fcDigits);
 654:     const cardCap = pow10(cardDigits);
 655:     const totalDecimal = fcCap * cardCap;
 656: 
 657:     const usableBits = Math.max(8, bits - 2);
 658:     const totalBinary = Math.pow(2, usableBits);
 659: 
 660:     const chosenTotal = fmt === "decimal" ? totalDecimal : totalBinary;
 661:     const utilization = chosenTotal > 0 && Number.isFinite(chosenTotal)
 662:       ? (population / chosenTotal) * 100
 663:       : 0;
 664: 
 665:     const result = classifyUtilization(utilization);
 666:     const formatLabel = fmt === "decimal" ? "Decimal" : "Binary";
 667:     const bestPractices = buildBestPractices();
 668: 
 669:     const rows = [
 670:       { label: "Format Type", value: formatLabel.toUpperCase() },
 671:       { label: "Badge Population", value: `${population}` },
 672:       { label: "Decimal Capacity (FC × Card)", value: `${formatNumber(totalDecimal)} (${formatNumber(fcCap)} × ${formatNumber(cardCap)})` },
 673:       { label: "Binary Capacity (approx)", value: `${formatNumber(totalBinary)} (usable bits ~ ${usableBits})` },
 674:       { label: "Capacity Used", value: `${utilization.toFixed(2)} %` },
 675:       { label: "Assessment", value: result.fit },
 676:       { label: "Engineering Interpretation", value: result.interpretation },
 677:       { label: "Best Practices", value: bestPractices }
 678:     ];
 679: 
 680:     render(rows);
 681: 
 682:     currentReport = buildReportPayload({
 683:       status: result.status,
 684:       summary: result.summary,
 685:       interpretation: result.interpretation,
 686:       inputs: {
 687:         fcDigits,
 688:         cardDigits,
 689:         formatLabel,
 690:         bits,
 691:         population
 692:       },
 693:       outputs: getRenderedRows()
 694:     });
 695: 
 696:     updateExportControls();
 697:   }
 698: 
 699:   function invalidate() {
 700:     currentReport = null;
 701: 
 702:     if (els.results) {
 703:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results.</div>`;
 704:     }
 705: 
 706:     updateExportControls();
 707:   }
 708: 
 709:   function reset() {
 710:     if (els.fcDigits) els.fcDigits.value = 3;
 711:     if (els.cardDigits) els.cardDigits.value = 5;
 712:     if (els.fmt) els.fmt.value = "decimal";
 713:     if (els.bits) els.bits.value = "26";
 714:     if (els.pop) els.pop.value = 500;
 715: 
 716:     currentReport = null;
 717: 
 718:     if (els.results) {
 719:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">Enter values and press Calculate.</div>`;
 720:     }
 721: 
 722:     updateExportControls();
 723:   }
 724: 
 725:   if (els.calc) {
 726:     els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);
 727:   }
 728: 
 729:   if (els.reset) {
 730:     els.reset.addEventListener("click", reset);
 731:   }
 732: 
 733:   [
 734:     els.fcDigits,
 735:     els.cardDigits,
 736:     els.fmt,
 737:     els.bits,
 738:     els.pop
 739:   ].forEach((el) => {
 740:     if (!el) return;
 741:     el.addEventListener("input", invalidate);
 742:     el.addEventListener("change", invalidate);
 743:   });
 744: 
 745:   [
 746:     els.reportTitle,
 747:     els.projectName,
 748:     els.clientName,
 749:     els.preparedBy,
 750:     els.customNotes
 751:   ].forEach((el) => {
 752:     if (!el) return;
 753:     el.addEventListener("input", () => {
 754:       if (!currentReport) return;
 755:       updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
 756:     });
 757:   });
 758: 
 759:   window.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
 760:     reset();
 761: 
 762:     setTimeout(() => {
 763:       updateExportControls();
 764:     }, 500);
 765:   });
 766: })();
 767: 


============================================================
TOOL: door-cable-length
============================================================
Title: Door Cable Length Estimator
Tier: pro
Meta description: Estimate realistic access-control door cable quantities and routing difficulty based on distance, slack, door count, and cable run strategy.
Flags: {
  "scriptJs": true,
  "pipeline": false,
  "flowNote": false,
  "continueButton": false,
  "exportCard": true,
  "helpJs": true,
  "analyzer": false
}

Input labels:
- Straight-Line Distance (ft)
- Routing Factor Light (open ceiling) ~15% Normal (mixed) ~30% Heavy (conduit/around obstacles) ~50%
- Service Slack (ft)
- Door Count
- Separate Runs? Single (combined cable) Multiple (reader + DPS + REX + lock)
- Number of Separate Cables (if multiple)
- Report Title
- Project Name
- Client Name
- Prepared By
- Custom Notes

Important IDs/names:
- viewport
- description

- distance
- routing
- slack
- doors

 306:   function collectVisibleResults() {
 307:     if (!els.results) return [];
 308: 
 309:     const rows = Array.from(els.results.querySelectorAll(".result-row"));
 310: 
 311:     return rows.map((rowEl) => {
 312:       const label = rowEl.querySelector(".result-label")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 313:       const value = rowEl.querySelector(".result-value")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 314:       return { label, value };
 315:     }).filter((item) => item.label && item.value);
 316:   }
 317: 
 318:   function getSummaryFromResults(outputs) {
 319:     const totalCable = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Estimated Total Cable")?.value || "";
 320:     const difficulty = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Install Difficulty")?.value || "";
 321:     const guidance = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Design Guidance")?.value || "";
 322: 
 323:     return `Estimated total cable is ${totalCable || "N/A"} with ${difficulty || "unknown"} install difficulty. ${guidance || ""}`.trim();
 324:   }
 325: 
 326:   function getInterpretationFromResults(outputs) {
 327:     return outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Engineering Insight")?.value || "";
 328:   }
 329: 
 330:   function getStatusFromResults(outputs) {
 331:     const difficulty = (outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Install Difficulty")?.value || "").toUpperCase();
 332: 
 333:     if (difficulty === "HIGH") return "RISK";
 334:     if (difficulty === "MODERATE") return "WATCH";
 335:     return "HEALTHY";
 336:   }

 342:       "This export reflects the current on-screen tool results at the time the report was opened or saved.",
 343:       "Final quantities should be verified against actual routing, pathway conditions, service loops, spare capacity, and installation standards."

 357:   function getExportChartImage() {
 358:     if (!lastMetrics || typeof Chart === "undefined") return getChartImage();
 359: 
 360:     try {
 361:       const canvas = document.createElement("canvas");
 362:       canvas.width = 1200;
 363:       canvas.height = 620;
 364: 
 365:       const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
 366:       if (!ctx) return getChartImage();
 367: 
 368:       const labels = [
 369:         "Per-Door Cable",
 370:         "Routing Loss %",
 371:         "Cable Density",
 372:         "Total Cable / 100"
 373:       ];
 374: 
 375:       const values = [
 376:         lastMetrics.perDoorTotal,
 377:         lastMetrics.routingLossPct,
 378:         lastMetrics.cableDensity * 40,
 379:         lastMetrics.totalAllDoors / 100
 380:       ];
 381: 
 382:       const displayNote = {
 383:         0: `${lastMetrics.perDoorTotal.toFixed(1)} ft`,
 384:         1: `${lastMetrics.routingLossPct.toFixed(0)}%`,
 385:         2: `${lastMetrics.cableDensity.toFixed(2)}`,
 386:         3: `${lastMetrics.totalAllDoors.toFixed(0)} ft total`
 387:       };
 388: 
 389:       const referenceValue = 220;
 390:       const dominantIndex = values.indexOf(Math.max(...values));
 391:       const maxValue = Math.max(...values, referenceValue, 300);
 392: 
 393:       let exportChart = null;
 394: 
 395:       const bgPlugin = {
 396:         id: "exportBgPlugin",
 397:         beforeDraw(chartInstance) {
 398:           const { ctx, chartArea } = chartInstance;
 399:           if (!chartArea) return;
 400: 
 401:           const { left, top, width, height, right, bottom } = chartArea;
 402:           const x = chartInstance.scales.x;
 403: 
 404:           ctx.save();
 405: 
 406:           ctx.fillStyle = "#ffffff";
 407:           ctx.fillRect(0, 0, chartInstance.width, chartInstance.height);
 408: 
 409:           ctx.fillStyle = "#f8fbf9";
 410:           ctx.fillRect(left, top, width, height);
 411: 
 412:           const healthyMax = Math.min(160, x.max);
 413:           const watchMax = Math.min(220, x.max);
 414: 
 415:           if (healthyMax > 0) {
 416:             ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.14)";
 417:             ctx.fillRect(left, top, x.getPixelForValue(healthyMax) - left, height);
 418:           }
 419: 
 420:           if (watchMax > 160) {
 421:             ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.14)";
 422:             ctx.fillRect(
 423:               x.getPixelForValue(160),
 424:               top,
 425:               x.getPixelForValue(watchMax) - x.getPixelForValue(160),
 426:               height
 427:             );
 428:           }
 429: 
 430:           if (x.max > 220) {
 431:             ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.12)";
 432:             ctx.fillRect(
 433:               x.getPixelForValue(220),
 434:               top,
 435:               right - x.getPixelForValue(220),
 436:               height
 437:             );
 438:           }
 439: 
 440:           ctx.restore();
 441:         },
 442:         afterDatasetsDraw(chartInstance) {
 443:           const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = chartInstance;
 444:           if (!chartArea || !scales.x || !scales.y) return;
 445: 
 446:           const x = scales.x;
 447:           const y = scales.y;
 448:           const { top, bottom } = chartArea;
 449: 
 450:           ctx.save();
 451: 
 452:           const rx = x.getPixelForValue(referenceValue);
 453:           ctx.strokeStyle = "#198754";
 454:           ctx.lineWidth = 3;
 455:           ctx.setLineDash([6, 5]);
 456:           ctx.beginPath();
 457:           ctx.moveTo(rx, top);
 458:           ctx.lineTo(rx, bottom);
 459:           ctx.stroke();
 460:           ctx.setLineDash([]);
 461: 
 462:           ctx.fillStyle = "#1f2937";
 463:           ctx.font = "600 16px Arial";
 464:           ctx.fillText("Install Watch Limit", rx + 10, bottom - 12);
 465: 
 466:           ctx.fillStyle = "#15803d";
 467:           ctx.font = "700 15px Arial";
 468:           ctx.fillText("Healthy", x.getPixelForValue(8), top + 18);
 469: 
 470:           ctx.fillStyle = "#b45309";
 471:           ctx.fillText("Watch", x.getPixelForValue(168), top + 18);
 472: 
 473:           ctx.fillStyle = "#b91c1c";
 474:           ctx.fillText("Risk", x.getPixelForValue(228), top + 18);
 475: 
 476:           const dominantValue = values[dominantIndex];
 477:           const px = x.getPixelForValue(dominantValue);
 478:           const py = y.getPixelForValue(labels[dominantIndex]);
 479: 
 480:           ctx.beginPath();
 481:           ctx.arc(px, py, 6, 0, Math.PI * 2);
 482:           ctx.fillStyle = "#ffffff";
 483:           ctx.fill();
 484:           ctx.strokeStyle = "#111827";
 485:           ctx.lineWidth = 2;
 486:           ctx.stroke();
 487: 
 488:           ctx.fillStyle = "#1f2937";
 489:           ctx.font = "600 15px Arial";
 490:           ctx.fillText(displayNote[dominantIndex], Math.min(px + 10, chartArea.right - 120), py - 10);
 491: 
 492:           ctx.restore();
 493:         }
 494:       };
 495: 
 496:       exportChart = new Chart(ctx, {
 497:         type: "bar",
 498:         data: {
 499:           labels,
 500:           datasets: [
 501:             {
 502:               label: "Cable Planning Metrics",
 503:               data: values,
 504:               indexAxis: "y",
 505:               barThickness: 18,
 506:               maxBarThickness: 18,
 507:               barPercentage: 0.8,
 508:               categoryPercentage: 0.7,
 509:               borderRadius: 8,
 510:               borderSkipped: false,
 511:               borderWidth: 1.5,
 512:               backgroundColor: (context) => {
 513:                 const i = context.dataIndex;
 514:                 const v = context.raw;
 515: 
 516:                 if (i === dominantIndex) {
 517:                   if (v > 220) return "#dc2626";
 518:                   if (v > 160) return "#f59e0b";
 519:                   return "#22c55e";
 520:                 }
 521: 
 522:                 if (v > 220) return "rgba(220, 38, 38, 0.55)";
 523:                 if (v > 160) return "rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.50)";
 524:                 return "rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.42)";

1023:   function getDifficulty(perDoorTotal, cableDensity, totalAllDoors) {
1024:     if (perDoorTotal > 350 || cableDensity > 3.2 || totalAllDoors > 4000) return "HIGH";
1025:     if (perDoorTotal > 220 || cableDensity > 2.0 || totalAllDoors > 2000) return "MODERATE";
1026:     return "LOW";
1027:   }
1028: 
1029:   function getRecommendation(difficulty, runs, distance) {
1030:     if (difficulty === "HIGH") {
1031:       return "Consider moving control hardware closer, reducing home-run distance, or splitting pathways by door group.";
1032:     }
1033: 
1034:     if (difficulty === "MODERATE") {
1035:       return "Routing is workable, but pathway efficiency, labeling, and slack discipline will matter in the field.";
1036:     }
1037: 
1038:     if (runs === "multi" && distance > 150) {
1039:       return "Runs are still acceptable, but verify pathway fill and service loop planning before rough-in.";
1040:     }
1041: 
1042:     return "Standard routing is acceptable.";
1043:   }
1044: 
1045:   function getInsight(difficulty) {
1046:     if (difficulty === "HIGH") {
1047:       return "Cable planning is entering a high-effort zone. Expect more labor, higher pathway congestion, and greater install/debug overhead if routing is not controlled carefully.";
1048:     }
1049: 
1050:     if (difficulty === "MODERATE") {
1051:       return "Cable design is reasonable, but not effortless. Installation success will depend on pathway cleanliness, termination consistency, and avoiding unnecessary reroutes.";
1052:     }
1053: 
1054:     return "Cable design is clean and efficient. Install should be straightforward with minimal overhead.";
1055:   }

1313:   function calc() {
1314:     const distance = Math.max(0, n("distance"));
1315:     const routing = parseFloat(els.routing.value);
1316:     const slack = Math.max(0, n("slack"));
1317:     const doors = Math.max(1, n("doors"));
1318:     const runs = els.runs.value;
1319:     const cables = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n("cables")));
1320: 
1321:     const routingFactor = Number.isFinite(routing) ? routing : 1.3;
1322:     const routed = distance * routingFactor;
1323:     const routingLossPct = (routingFactor - 1) * 100;
1324:     const perDoorSingle = routed + slack;
1325:     const perDoorTotal = runs === "multi" ? perDoorSingle * cables : perDoorSingle;
1326:     const totalAllDoors = perDoorTotal * doors;
1327:     const cableDensity = perDoorTotal / Math.max(1, distance);
1328: 
1329:     const difficulty = getDifficulty(perDoorTotal, cableDensity, totalAllDoors);
1330:     const recommendation = getRecommendation(difficulty, runs, distance);
1331:     const insight = getInsight(difficulty);
1332: 
1333:     els.results.innerHTML = [
1334:       row("Routed Distance (per door)", `${routed.toFixed(1)} ft`),
1335:       row("Routing Loss", `${routingLossPct.toFixed(0)}%`),
1336:       row("Estimated Run (single cable)", `${perDoorSingle.toFixed(1)} ft`),
1337:       row("Estimated Total per Door", `${perDoorTotal.toFixed(1)} ft`),
1338:       row("Estimated Total Cable", `${totalAllDoors.toFixed(1)} ft`),
1339:       row("Cable Density", cableDensity.toFixed(2)),
1340:       row("Install Difficulty", difficulty),
1341:       row("Design Guidance", recommendation),
1342:       row("Engineering Insight", insight)
1343:     ].join("");
1344: 
1345:     lastMetrics = {
1346:       perDoorTotal,
1347:       routingLossPct,
1348:       cableDensity,
1349:       totalAllDoors
1350:     };
1351: 
1352:     renderChart(lastMetrics);
1353: 
1354:     currentReport = buildCurrentReportPayload();
1355:     updateExportControls();
1356:   }
1357:

1359:     if (els.results) {
1360:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>`;
1361:     }
1362: 
1363:     destroyChart();
1364:     lastMetrics = null;
1365:     currentReport = null;
1366:     updateExportControls();

1378:     if (els.runs) els.runs.value = "single";

 297:   function saveSnapshotToStorage(key, payload, limit = 25) {
 298:     const existing = readSnapshots(key);
 299: 
 300:     existing.unshift({
 301:       ...payload,
 302:       savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
 303:     });
 304: 
 305:     const trimmed = existing.slice(0, limit);
 306:     writeSnapshots(key, trimmed);
 307: 
 308:     return trimmed.length;
 309:   }

 998:   function openReportWindow(payload) {
 999:     try {
1000:       const html = buildReportHTML(payload);
1001:       const blob = new Blob([html], { type: "text/html" });
1002:       const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
1003:       const win = window.open(url, "_blank");
1004: 
1005:       if (!win) return false;
1006: 
1007:       setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 10000);
1008:       return true;
1009:     } catch (err) {
1010:       console.error("Export report open failed:", err);
1011:       return false;
1012:     }
1013:   }

1015:   function getStatus(complexityIndex) {
1016:     if (complexityIndex > 140) return "RISK";
1017:     if (complexityIndex > 80) return "WATCH";
1018:     return "HEALTHY";
1019:   }

1021:   function getGuidance(status) {
1022:     if (status === "RISK") {
1023:       return "System is becoming complex. Consider segmentation strategy, controller distribution, and phased deployment.";
1024:     }
1025: 
1026:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1027:       return "System complexity is rising. Ensure controller placement and wiring paths are well planned.";
1028:     }
1029: 
1030:     return "Standard segmentation is acceptable.";
1031:   }
1032: 
1033:   function getInsight(status) {
1034:     if (status === "RISK") {
1035:       return "High door count and segmentation will increase install time, wiring complexity, and long-term management overhead.";
1036:     }
1037: 
1038:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1039:       return "System is manageable but requires disciplined layout and clear segmentation boundaries.";
1040:     }
1041: 
1042:     return "System is clean and scalable with minimal administrative overhead.";
1043:   }

1045:   function renderChart(data) {
1046:     destroyChart();
1047: 
1048:     if (!els.chart) return;
1049: 
1050:     showChartWrap();
1051: 
1052:     const labels = [
1053:       "Doors",
1054:       "Zones Impact",
1055:       "Readers",
1056:       "Complexity"
1057:     ];
1058: 
1059:     const values = [
1060:       data.doors,
1061:       data.zonesImpact,
1062:       data.readers,
1063:       data.complexityIndex
1064:     ];
1065: 
1066:     const displayValues = {
1067:       0: `${data.doors} doors`,
1068:       1: `${data.zonesImpact} impact`,
1069:       2: `${data.readers} readers`,
1070:       3: `${data.complexityIndex} complexity`
1071:     };
1072: 
1073:     const dominantIndex = values.indexOf(Math.max(...values));
1074:     const referenceValue = 80;
1075:     const chartMax = Math.max(160, Math.ceil(Math.max(...values, referenceValue, 140) * 1.12));
1076: 
1077:     const chartBgPlugin = {
1078:       id: "chartBgPlugin",
1079:       beforeDraw(c) {
1080:         const { ctx, chartArea } = c;
1081:         if (!chartArea) return;
1082: 
1083:         const { left, top, width, height } = chartArea;
1084: 
1085:         ctx.save();
1086:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255,255,255,0.05)";
1087:         ctx.fillRect(left, top, width, height);
1088:         ctx.restore();
1089:       }
1090:     };
1091: 
1092:     const thresholdBandPlugin = {
1093:       id: "thresholdBandPlugin",
1094:       beforeDatasetsDraw(c) {
1095:         const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = c;
1096:         if (!chartArea || !scales.x) return;
1097: 
1098:         const x = scales.x;
1099:         const { top, bottom, left, right } = chartArea;
1100: 
1101:         const healthyMax = Math.min(80, x.max);
1102:         const watchMax = Math.min(140, x.max);
1103: 
1104:         ctx.save();
1105: 
1106:         if (healthyMax > 0) {
1107:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(46, 204, 113, 0.16)";
1108:           ctx.fillRect(left, top, x.getPixelForValue(healthyMax) - left, bottom - top);
1109:         }
1110: 
1111:         if (watchMax > 80) {
1112:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 200, 80, 0.13)";
1113:           ctx.fillRect(
1114:             x.getPixelForValue(80),
1115:             top,
1116:             x.getPixelForValue(watchMax) - x.getPixelForValue(80),
1117:             bottom - top
1118:           );
1119:         }
1120: 
1121:         if (x.max > 140) {
1122:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 90, 90, 0.13)";
1123:           ctx.fillRect(
1124:             x.getPixelForValue(140),
1125:             top,
1126:             right - x.getPixelForValue(140),
1127:             bottom - top
1128:           );
1129:         }
1130: 
1131:         ctx.restore();
1132:       },
1133:       afterDatasetsDraw(c) {
1134:         const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = c;
1135:         if (!chartArea || !scales.x || !scales.y) return;
1136: 
1137:         const x = scales.x;
1138:         const y = scales.y;
1139:         const { top, bottom } = chartArea;
1140: 
1141:         ctx.save();
1142: 
1143:         const rx = x.getPixelForValue(referenceValue);
1144:         ctx.strokeStyle = "rgba(120, 255, 170, 0.98)";
1145:         ctx.lineWidth = 3;
1146:         ctx.setLineDash([4, 4]);
1147:         ctx.beginPath();
1148:         ctx.moveTo(rx, top);
1149:         ctx.lineTo(rx, bottom);
1150:         ctx.stroke();
1151:         ctx.setLineDash([]);
1152: 
1153:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(220, 255, 235, 0.96)";
1154:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1155:         ctx.fillText("Complexity Watch Limit", rx + 8, bottom - 10);
1156: 
1157:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(180, 255, 200, 0.82)";
1158:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1159:         ctx.fillText("Healthy", x.getPixelForValue(8), top + 14);
1160: 
1161:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 220, 140, 0.82)";
1162:         ctx.fillText("Watch", x.getPixelForValue(88), top + 14);
1163: 
1164:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 160, 160, 0.82)";
1165:         ctx.fillText("Risk", x.getPixelForValue(148), top + 14);
1166: 
1167:         const dominantValue = values[dominantIndex];
1168:         const px = x.getPixelForValue(dominantValue);
1169:         const py = y.getPixelForValue(labels[dominantIndex]);
1170: 
1171:         ctx.beginPath();
1172:         ctx.arc(px, py, 4.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
1173:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(225, 255, 240, 1)";
1174:         ctx.fill();
1175:         ctx.strokeStyle = "rgba(120, 255, 170, 0.95)";
1176:         ctx.lineWidth = 2;
1177:         ctx.stroke();
1178: 
1179:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(235, 248, 240, 0.92)";
1180:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1181:         ctx.fillText(displayValues[dominantIndex], Math.min(px + 8, chartArea.right - 110), py - 8);
1182: 
1183:         ctx.restore();
1184:       }
1185:     };
1186: 
1187:     chart = new Chart(els.chart, {
1188:       type: "bar",
1189:       data: {
1190:         labels,
1191:         datasets: [
1192:           {
1193:             label: "Door Planning Metrics",
1194:             data: values,
1195:             barThickness: 16,
1196:             maxBarThickness: 16,
1197:             barPercentage: 0.8,
1198:             categoryPercentage: 0.7,
1199:             borderWidth: 2,
1200:             borderRadius: 8,
1201:             borderSkipped: false,
1202:             backgroundColor: (context) => {
1203:               const i = context.dataIndex;
1204:               const v = context.raw;
1205: 
1206:               if (i === dominantIndex) {
1207:                 if (v > 140) return "rgba(255, 92, 92, 1)";
1208:                 if (v > 80) return "rgba(255, 188, 82, 1)";
1209:                 return "rgba(120, 255, 170, 1)";
1210:               }
1211: 
1212:               if (v > 140) return "rgba(255, 77, 77, 0.30)";
1213:               if (v > 80) return "rgba(255, 170, 51, 0.24)";
1214:               return "rgba(90, 170, 255, 0.15)";
1215:             },

--- CORE BLOCK 7 ---
1260:               }
1261:             }
1262:           }
1263:         },
1264:         scales: {
1265:           x: {
1266:             beginAtZero: true,
1267:             suggestedMax: chartMax,
1268:             ticks: {
1269:               color: "rgba(220, 238, 230, 0.78)"
1270:             },
1271:             grid: {
1272:               color: "rgba(110, 160, 140, 0.10)"
1273:             },
1274:             title: {
1275:               display: true,
1276:               text: "Planning Magnitude",
1277:               color: "rgba(230, 255, 240, 0.92)"
1278:             }
1279:           },
1280:           y: {
1281:             ticks: {
1282:               color: "rgba(228, 245, 235, 0.92)"
1283:             },
1284:             grid: {
1285:               display: false
1286:             }
1287:           }
1288:         }
1289:       },
1290:       plugins: [chartBgPlugin, thresholdBandPlugin]
1291:     });

1301:   function calc() {
1302:     const perimeter = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("perimeter")));
1303:     const zones = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("zones")));
1304:     const highsec = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("highsec")));
1305:     const compliance = els.compliance.value;
1306:     const bothSides = els.bothSides.value;
1307: 
1308:     const perimeterDoors = perimeter;
1309:     const zoneBase = zones * 1.6 * compFactor(compliance);
1310:     const highsecAdd = highsec * (compliance === "strict" ? 2.0 : 1.3);
1311: 
1312:     let doors = Math.round(perimeterDoors + zoneBase + highsecAdd);
1313:     doors = Math.max(0, doors);
1314: 
1315:     const readerMultiplier = bothSides === "yes" ? 2 : 1;
1316:     const readers = doors * readerMultiplier;
1317: 
1318:     const zonesImpact = Math.round(zones * 5);
1319:     const complexityIndex = Math.round(
1320:       doors +
1321:       zones * 2 +
1322:       highsec * 5 +
1323:       (bothSides === "yes" ? doors * 0.5 : 0)
1324:     );
1325: 
1326:     const status = getStatus(complexityIndex);
1327:     const guidance = getGuidance(status);
1328:     const insight = getInsight(status);
1329: 
1330:     els.results.innerHTML = [
1331:       row("Perimeter Doors", perimeterDoors),
1332:       row("Interior Zone Doors", Math.round(zoneBase)),
1333:       row("High-Security Additions", Math.round(highsecAdd)),
1334:       row("Total Controlled Doors", doors),
1335:       row("Estimated Reader Count", readers),
1336:       row("Complexity Index", complexityIndex),
1337:       row("System Status", status),
1338:       row("Design Guidance", guidance),
1339:       row("Engineering Insight", insight)
1340:     ].join("");
1341: 
1342:     lastMetrics = {
1343:       doors,
1344:       zonesImpact,
1345:       readers,
1346:       complexityIndex
1347:     };
1348: 
1349:     renderChart(lastMetrics);
1350: 
1351:     currentReport = buildCurrentReportPayload();
1352:     updateExportControls();
1353:   }
1354: 
1355:   function resetResults(message = "Enter values and press Calculate.") {
1356:     if (els.results) {
1357:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>`;
1358:     }
1359: 
1360:     destroyChart();
1361:     lastMetrics = null;
1362:     currentReport = null;
1363:     updateExportControls();
1364:   }
1365: 
1366:   function invalidate() {
1367:     resetResults("Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results.");
1368:   }
1369: 
1370:   function reset() {
1371:     if (els.perimeter) els.perimeter.value = 8;
1372:     if (els.zones) els.zones.value = 6;
1373:     if (els.highsec) els.highsec.value = 2;
1374:     if (els.compliance) els.compliance.value = "basic";
1375:     if (els.bothSides) els.bothSides.value = "no";
1376: 
1377:     resetResults("Enter values and press Calculate.");
1378:   }
1379: 
1380:   if (els.calc) {
1381:     els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);
1382:   }
1383: 
1384:   if (els.reset) {
1385:     els.reset.addEventListener("click", reset);
1386:   }
1387: 
1388:   [
1389:     els.perimeter,
1390:     els.zones,
1391:     els.highsec,
1392:     els.compliance,
1393:     els.bothSides
1394:   ].forEach((el) => {
1395:     if (!el) return;
1396:     el.addEventListener("input", invalidate);
1397:     el.addEventListener("change", invalidate);
1398:   });
1399: 
1400:   [
1401:     els.reportTitle,
1402:     els.projectName,
1403:     els.clientName,
1404:     els.preparedBy,
1405:     els.customNotes
1406:   ].forEach((el) => {
1407:     if (!el) return;
1408:     el.addEventListener("input", () => {
1409:       if (!currentReport) return;
1410:       updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
1411:     });
1412:   });
1413: 
1414:   if (els.chart) {
1415:     els.chart.style.width = "100%";
1416:     els.chart.style.height = "340px";
1417: 
1418:     if (els.chart.parentElement) {
1419:       els.chart.parentElement.style.minHeight = "340px";
1420:     }
1421:   }
1422: 
1423:   reset();
1424: })();

 291:   function saveSnapshotToStorage(key, payload, limit = 25) {
 292:     const existing = readSnapshots(key);
 293: 
 294:     existing.unshift({
 295:       ...payload,
 296:       savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
 297:     });
 298: 
 299:     const trimmed = existing.slice(0, limit);
 300:     writeSnapshots(key, trimmed);
 301: 
 302:     return trimmed.length;
 303:   }

 305:   function collectVisibleResults() {
 306:     if (!els.results) return [];
 307: 
 308:     const rows = Array.from(els.results.querySelectorAll(".result-row"));
 309: 
 310:     return rows.map((rowEl) => {
 311:       const label = rowEl.querySelector(".result-label")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 312:       const value = rowEl.querySelector(".result-value")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 313:       return { label, value };
 314:     }).filter((item) => item.label && item.value);
 315:   }
 316: 
 317:   function getSummaryFromResults(outputs) {
 318:     const totalReaders = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Estimated Total Readers")?.value || "";
 319:     const status = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "System Status")?.value || "";
 320:     const placement = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Placement")?.value || "";
 321: 
 322:     return `Estimated elevator access design requires ${totalReaders || "N/A"} readers with ${status || "unknown"} system status using a ${placement || "N/A"} placement strategy.`;
 323:   }
 324: 
 325:   function getInterpretationFromResults(outputs) {
 326:     return outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Engineering Insight")?.value || "";
 327:   }
 328: 
 329:   function getStatusFromResults(outputs) {
 330:     const status = (outputs.find((x) => x.label === "System Status")?.value || "").toUpperCase();
 331: 
 332:     if (status === "RISK") return "RISK";
 333:     if (status === "WATCH") return "WATCH";
 334:     return "HEALTHY";
 335:   }

 341:       "Outputs are planning aids for hardware and integration magnitude, not controller-specific elevator interface sizing.",
 342:       "Elevator access design should be validated with the elevator contractor, access-control platform, fire/life-safety requirements, override behavior, and owner operating policy."
 343:     ];

 350:       }
 351:     } catch {}

 356:   function getExportChartImage() {
 357:     if (!lastMetrics || typeof Chart === "undefined") return getChartImage();
 358: 
 359:     try {
 360:       const canvas = document.createElement("canvas");
 361:       canvas.width = 1200;
 362:       canvas.height = 620;
 363: 
 364:       const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
 365:       if (!ctx) return getChartImage();
 366: 
 367:       const labels = [
 368:         "Total Readers",
 369:         "Cars Impact",
 370:         "Lobby Impact",
 371:         "Complexity"
 372:       ];
 373: 
 374:       const values = [
 375:         lastMetrics.totalReaders,
 376:         lastMetrics.carReaders,
 377:         lastMetrics.lobbyReaders + lastMetrics.dcsAdd,
 378:         lastMetrics.complexityIndex
 379:       ];
 380: 
 381:       const displayValues = {
 382:         0: `${lastMetrics.totalReaders} readers`,
 383:         1: `${lastMetrics.carReaders} in-car`,
 384:         2: `${lastMetrics.lobbyReaders + lastMetrics.dcsAdd} lobby/DCS`,
 385:         3: `${lastMetrics.complexityIndex} complexity`
 386:       };
 387: 
 388:       const referenceValue = 30;
 389:       const dominantIndex = values.indexOf(Math.max(...values));
 390:       const maxValue = Math.max(...values, referenceValue, 100);
 391: 
 392:       let exportChart = null;
 393: 
 394:       const bgPlugin = {
 395:         id: "exportBgPlugin",
 396:         beforeDraw(chartInstance) {
 397:           const { ctx, chartArea } = chartInstance;
 398:           if (!chartArea) return;
 399: 
 400:           const { left, top, width, height, right, bottom } = chartArea;
 401:           const x = chartInstance.scales.x;
 402: 
 403:           ctx.save();
 404: 
 405:           ctx.fillStyle = "#ffffff";
 406:           ctx.fillRect(0, 0, chartInstance.width, chartInstance.height);
 407: 
 408:           ctx.fillStyle = "#f8fbf9";
 409:           ctx.fillRect(left, top, width, height);
 410: 
 411:           const healthyMax = Math.min(30, x.max);
 412:           const watchMax = Math.min(55, x.max);
 413: 
 414:           if (healthyMax > 0) {
 415:             ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(34, 197, 94, 0.14)";
 416:             ctx.fillRect(left, top, x.getPixelForValue(healthyMax) - left, height);
 417:           }
 418: 
 419:           if (watchMax > 30) {
 420:             ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.14)";
 421:             ctx.fillRect(
 422:               x.getPixelForValue(30),
 423:               top,
 424:               x.getPixelForValue(watchMax) - x.getPixelForValue(30),
 425:               height
 426:             );
 427:           }
 428: 
 429:           if (x.max > 55) {
 430:             ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.12)";
 431:             ctx.fillRect(
 432:               x.getPixelForValue(55),
 433:               top,
 434:               right - x.getPixelForValue(55),
 435:               height
 436:             );
 437:           }
 438: 
 439:           ctx.restore();
 440:         },
 441:         afterDatasetsDraw(chartInstance) {
 442:           const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = chartInstance;
 443:           if (!chartArea || !scales.x || !scales.y) return;
 444: 
 445:           const x = scales.x;
 446:           const y = scales.y;
 447:           const { top, bottom } = chartArea;
 448: 
 449:           ctx.save();
 450: 
 451:           const rx = x.getPixelForValue(referenceValue);
 452:           ctx.strokeStyle = "#198754";
 453:           ctx.lineWidth = 3;
 454:           ctx.setLineDash([6, 5]);
 455:           ctx.beginPath();
 456:           ctx.moveTo(rx, top);
 457:           ctx.lineTo(rx, bottom);
 458:           ctx.stroke();
 459:           ctx.setLineDash([]);
 460: 
 461:           ctx.fillStyle = "#1f2937";
 462:           ctx.font = "600 16px Arial";
 463:           ctx.fillText("Planning Watch Limit", rx + 10, bottom - 12);
 464: 
 465:           ctx.fillStyle = "#15803d";
 466:           ctx.font = "700 15px Arial";
 467:           ctx.fillText("Healthy", x.getPixelForValue(4), top + 18);
 468: 
 469:           ctx.fillStyle = "#b45309";
 470:           ctx.fillText("Watch", x.getPixelForValue(34), top + 18);
 471: 
 472:           ctx.fillStyle = "#b91c1c";
 473:           ctx.fillText("Risk", x.getPixelForValue(59), top + 18);
 474: 
 475:           const dominantValue = values[dominantIndex];
 476:           const px = x.getPixelForValue(dominantValue);
 477:           const py = y.getPixelForValue(labels[dominantIndex]);
 478: 
 479:           ctx.beginPath();
 480:           ctx.arc(px, py, 6, 0, Math.PI * 2);
 481:           ctx.fillStyle = "#ffffff";
 482:           ctx.fill();
 483:           ctx.strokeStyle = "#111827";
 484:           ctx.lineWidth = 2;
 485:           ctx.stroke();
 486: 
 487:           ctx.fillStyle = "#1f2937";
 488:           ctx.font = "600 15px Arial";
 489:           ctx.fillText(displayValues[dominantIndex], Math.min(px + 10, chartArea.right - 120), py - 10);
 490: 
 491:           ctx.restore();
 492:         }
 493:       };
 494: 
 495:       exportChart = new Chart(ctx, {
 496:         type: "bar",
 497:         data: {
 498:           labels,
 499:           datasets: [
 500:             {
 501:               label: "Elevator Reader Metrics",
 502:               data: values,
 503:               indexAxis: "y",
 504:               barThickness: 18,
 505:               maxBarThickness: 18,
 506:               barPercentage: 0.8,
 507:               categoryPercentage: 0.7,
 508:               borderRadius: 8,
 509:               borderSkipped: false,
 510:               borderWidth: 1.5,
 511:               backgroundColor: (context) => {
 512:                 const i = context.dataIndex;
 513:                 const v = context.raw;
 514: 
 515:                 if (i === dominantIndex) {
 516:                   if (v > 55) return "#dc2626";
 517:                   if (v > 30) return "#f59e0b";
 518:                   return "#22c55e";
 519:                 }
 520: 
 521:                 if (v > 55) return "rgba(220, 38, 38, 0.55)";
 522:                 if (v > 30) return "rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.50)";
 523:                 return "rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.42)";

 992:   function openReportWindow(payload) {
 993:     try {
 994:       const html = buildReportHTML(payload);
 995:       const blob = new Blob([html], { type: "text/html" });
 996:       const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);

 998:

1002:       return true;
1003:     } catch (err) {

1005:       return false;

1019:   function getGuidance(status, placement, dest) {
1020:     if (status === "RISK") {
1021:       return "Reader strategy is becoming complex. Coordinate early with the elevator contractor and validate kiosk, car, and override behaviors before procurement.";
1022:     }
1023: 
1024:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1025:       return "Design is workable, but integration detail matters. Confirm reader placement, throughput expectations, and emergency override sequences.";
1026:     }
1027: 
1028:     if (dest === "yes" && placement === "car") {
1029:       return "DCS is present, so verify whether lobby authentication is actually required before locking into in-car-only hardware.";
1030:     }
1031: 
1032:     return "Reader strategy is straightforward and should deploy cleanly with normal coordination.";
1033:   }

1035:   function getInsight(status, dest, total) {
1036:     if (status === "RISK") {
1037:       return `This elevator access design is hardware-heavy. At ${total} estimated readers, the challenge is less about count and more about integration behavior, queue flow, and how cleanly elevator logic is coordinated with access control.`;
1038:     }
1039: 
1040:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1041:       return "This is a moderate-complexity elevator access design. Hardware count is manageable, but reader location and user flow will determine whether the system feels smooth or frustrating in daily use.";
1042:     }
1043: 
1044:     if (dest === "yes") {
1045:       return "The reader count remains reasonable, but DCS changes where authentication belongs. Keep user interaction aligned with the destination-selection point, not just the elevator car.";
1046:     }
1047: 
1048:     return "This is a clean elevator reader design with limited deployment overhead and predictable control behavior.";
1049:   }

1051:   function renderChart(data) {

1075:       2: `${data.lobbyReaders + data.dcsAdd} lobby/DCS`,
1076:       3: `${data.complexityIndex} complexity`
1077:     };
1078: 
1079:     const dominantIndex = values.indexOf(Math.max(...values));
1080:     const referenceValue = 30;
1081:     const chartMax = Math.max(100, Math.ceil(Math.max(...values, referenceValue, 60) * 1.12));
1082: 
1083:     const chartBgPlugin = {
1084:       id: "chartBgPlugin",
1085:       beforeDraw(c) {
1086:         const { ctx, chartArea } = c;
1087:         if (!chartArea) return;
1088: 
1089:         const { left, top, width, height } = chartArea;
1090: 
1091:         ctx.save();
1092:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255,255,255,0.05)";

1094:         ctx.restore();
1095:       }
1096:     };
1097: 
1098:     const thresholdBandPlugin = {
1099:       id: "thresholdBandPlugin",
1100:       beforeDatasetsDraw(c) {
1101:         const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = c;
1102:         if (!chartArea || !scales.x) return;
1103: 
1104:         const x = scales.x;
1105:         const { top, bottom, left, right } = chartArea;
1106: 
1107:         const healthyMax = Math.min(30, x.max);
1108:         const watchMax = Math.min(55, x.max);
1109: 
1110:         ctx.save();
1111: 
1112:         if (healthyMax > 0) {
1113:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(46, 204, 113, 0.16)";
1114:           ctx.fillRect(left, top, x.getPixelForValue(healthyMax) - left, bottom - top);
1115:         }
1116: 
1117:         if (watchMax > 30) {
1118:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 200, 80, 0.13)";
1119:           ctx.fillRect(
1120:             x.getPixelForValue(30),
1121:             top,
1122:             x.getPixelForValue(watchMax) - x.getPixelForValue(30),
1123:             bottom - top
1124:           );
1125:         }
1126: 
1127:         if (x.max > 55) {
1128:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 90, 90, 0.13)";
1129:           ctx.fillRect(
1130:             x.getPixelForValue(55),
1131:             top,
1132:             right - x.getPixelForValue(55),
1133:             bottom - top
1134:           );
1135:         }
1136: 
1137:         ctx.restore();
1138:       },
1139:       afterDatasetsDraw(c) {
1140:         const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = c;
1141:         if (!chartArea || !scales.x || !scales.y) return;
1142: 
1143:         const x = scales.x;
1144:         const y = scales.y;
1145:         const { top, bottom } = chartArea;
1146: 
1147:         ctx.save();
1148: 
1149:         const rx = x.getPixelForValue(referenceValue);
1150:         ctx.strokeStyle = "rgba(120, 255, 170, 0.98)";
1151:         ctx.lineWidth = 3;
1152:         ctx.setLineDash([4, 4]);
1153:         ctx.beginPath();
1154:         ctx.moveTo(rx, top);
1155:         ctx.lineTo(rx, bottom);
1156:         ctx.stroke();
1157:         ctx.setLineDash([]);
1158: 
1159:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(220, 255, 235, 0.96)";
1160:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1161:         ctx.fillText("Planning Watch Limit", rx + 8, bottom - 10);
1162: 
1163:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(180, 255, 200, 0.82)";
1164:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1165:         ctx.fillText("Healthy", x.getPixelForValue(4), top + 14);
1166: 
1167:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 220, 140, 0.82)";
1168:         ctx.fillText("Watch", x.getPixelForValue(34), top + 14);
1169: 
1170:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 160, 160, 0.82)";
1171:         ctx.fillText("Risk", x.getPixelForValue(59), top + 14);

1174:         const px = x.getPixelForValue(dominantValue);
1175:         const py = y.getPixelForValue(labels[dominantIndex]);
1176: 
1177:         ctx.beginPath();

1179:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(225, 255, 240, 1)";
1180:         ctx.fill();
1181:         ctx.strokeStyle = "rgba(120, 255, 170, 0.95)";
1182:         ctx.lineWidth = 2;
1183:         ctx.stroke();

1186:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1187:         ctx.fillText(displayValues[dominantIndex], Math.min(px + 8, chartArea.right - 110), py - 8);
1188: 
1189:         ctx.restore();
1190:       }
1191:     };

1307:   function calc() {
1308:     const cars = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("cars")));
1309:     const banks = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n("banks")));
1310:     const floors = Math.max(0, Math.floor(n("floors")));
1311:     const dest = els.dest.value;
1312:     const placement = els.placement.value;
1313: 
1314:     if (cars <= 0) {
1315:       if (els.results) {
1316:         els.results.innerHTML = row("Error", "Enter Elevator Cars > 0");
1317:       }
1318: 
1319:       destroyChart();
1320:       lastMetrics = null;
1321:       currentReport = null;
1322:       updateExportControls();
1323:       return;
1324:     }
1325: 
1326:     let carReaders = 0;
1327:     let lobbyReaders = 0;
1328: 
1329:     if (placement === "car") {
1330:       carReaders = cars;
1331:     } else if (placement === "lobby") {
1332:       lobbyReaders = banks * getPerBankReaders(floors);
1333:     } else {
1334:       carReaders = cars;
1335:       lobbyReaders = banks * getPerBankReaders(floors);
1336:     }
1337: 
1338:     let dcsAdd = 0;
1339: 
1340:     if (dest === "yes") {
1341:       if (placement === "lobby" || placement === "both") {
1342:         dcsAdd = banks;
1343:       } else {
1344:         dcsAdd = Math.max(1, Math.round(banks * 0.5));
1345:       }
1346:     }
1347: 
1348:     const totalReaders = carReaders + lobbyReaders + dcsAdd;
1349: 
1350:     const complexityIndex = Math.round(
1351:       totalReaders +
1352:       floors * 1.5 +
1353:       banks * 4 +
1354:       (dest === "yes" ? 12 : 0) +
1355:       (placement === "both" ? 10 : placement === "lobby" ? 4 : 0)
1356:     );
1357: 
1358:     const status = getStatus(complexityIndex);
1359:     const guidance = getGuidance(status, placement, dest);
1360:     const insight = getInsight(status, dest, totalReaders);
1361: 
1362:     els.results.innerHTML = [
1363:       row("Cars", cars),
1364:       row("Banks", banks),
1365:       row("Secured Floors", floors),
1366:       row("Destination Control", dest === "yes" ? "YES" : "NO"),
1367:       row("Placement", placement.toUpperCase()),
1368:       row("Car Readers (est.)", carReaders),
1369:       row("Lobby Readers (est.)", lobbyReaders),
1370:       row("DCS Adders (est.)", dcsAdd),
1371:       row("Estimated Total Readers", totalReaders),
1372:       row("Planning Complexity", complexityIndex),
1373:       row("System Status", status),
1374:       row("Design Guidance", guidance),
1375:       row("Engineering Insight", insight)
1376:     ].join("");
1377: 
1378:     lastMetrics = {
1379:       totalReaders,
1380:       carReaders,
1381:       lobbyReaders,
1382:       dcsAdd,
1383:       complexityIndex
1384:     };
1385: 
1386:     renderChart(lastMetrics);
1387: 
1388:     currentReport = buildCurrentReportPayload();
1389:     updateExportControls();
1390:   }
1391: 
1392:   function resetResults(message = "Enter values and press Calculate.") {
1393:     if (els.results) {
1394:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>`;
1395:     }
1396: 
1397:     destroyChart();
1398:     lastMetrics = null;
1399:     currentReport = null;
1400:     updateExportControls();
1401:   }
1402: 
1403:   function invalidate() {
1404:     resetResults("Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results.");
1405:   }
1406: 
1407:   function reset() {
1408:     if (els.cars) els.cars.value = 6;
1409:     if (els.banks) els.banks.value = 2;
1410:     if (els.floors) els.floors.value = 8;
1411:     if (els.dest) els.dest.value = "no";
1412:     if (els.placement) els.placement.value = "car";
1413: 
1414:     resetResults("Enter values and press Calculate.");
1415:   }
1416: 
1417:   if (els.calc) {
1418:     els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);
1419:   }
1420: 
1421:   if (els.reset) {
1422:     els.reset.addEventListener("click", reset);
1423:   }
1424: 
1425:   [
1426:     els.cars,
1427:     els.banks,
1428:     els.floors,
1429:     els.dest,
1430:     els.placement
1431:   ].forEach((el) => {
1432:     if (!el) return;
1433:     el.addEventListener("input", invalidate);
1434:     el.addEventListener("change", invalidate);
1435:   });
1436: 
1437:   [
1438:     els.reportTitle,
1439:     els.projectName,
1440:     els.clientName,
1441:     els.preparedBy,
1442:     els.customNotes
1443:   ].forEach((el) => {
1444:     if (!el) return;
1445:     el.addEventListener("input", () => {
1446:       if (!currentReport) return;
1447:       updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
1448:     });
1449:   });
1450: 
1451:   if (els.chart) {
1452:     els.chart.style.width = "100%";
1453:     els.chart.style.height = "340px";
1454: 
1455:     if (els.chart.parentElement) {
1456:       els.chart.parentElement.style.minHeight = "340px";
1457:     }
1458:   }
1459: 
1460:   reset();
1461: })();

 285:   function getRenderedRows() {
 286:     if (!els.results) return [];
 287: 
 288:     return Array.from(els.results.querySelectorAll(".result-row"))
 289:       .map((row) => {
 290:         const label = row.querySelector(".result-label")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 291:         const value = row.querySelector(".result-value")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 292:         return { label, value };
 293:       })
 294:       .filter((item) => item.label || item.value);
 295:   }
 296: 
 297:   function readSnapshots(key) {
 298:     try {
 299:       const raw = localStorage.getItem(key);
 300:       const parsed = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : [];
 301:       return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
 302:     } catch {
 303:       return [];
 304:     }
 305:   }
 306: 
 307:   function writeSnapshots(key, items) {
 308:     localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items));
 309:   }

 693:   function savePipelineResult(payload) {
 694:     ScopedLabsAnalyzer.writeFlow(FLOW_KEYS[STEP], {
 695:       category: CATEGORY,
 696:       step: STEP,
 697:       lane: LANE,
 698:       data: payload
 699:     });
 700:   }
 701: 
 702:   function invalidatePipelineResult() {
 703:     try {
 704:       Object.values(FLOW_KEYS).forEach((key) => {
 705:         sessionStorage.removeItem(key);
 706:       });
 707:     } catch {}
 708: 
 709:     hideContinue();
 710:   }
 711: 
 712:   function clearAnalysis() {
 713:     if (window.ScopedLabsAnalyzer && els.analysis) {
 714:       ScopedLabsAnalyzer.clearAnalysisBlock(els.analysis);
 715:     } else if (els.analysis) {
 716:       els.analysis.innerHTML = "";
 717:       els.analysis.style.display = "none";
 718:     }
 719:   }
 720: 
 721:   function clearResults(message = "Run the evaluation to see results.") {
 722:     if (els.results) {
 723:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>`;
 724:     }
 725: 
 726:     clearAnalysis();
 727:     hideContinue();
 728:   }
 729: 
 730:   function invalidate() {
 731:     currentReport = null;
 732:     invalidatePipelineResult();
 733:     clearResults("Inputs changed. Press Evaluate to refresh results.");
 734:     updateExportControls();
 735:   }
 736: 
 737:   function getConfidence(score) {
 738:     const abs = Math.abs(score);
 739:     if (abs >= 4) return "HIGH";
 740:     if (abs >= 2) return "MEDIUM";
 741:     return "LOW";
 742:   }
 743: 
 744:   function getScoreMeaning(score) {
 745:     if (score >= 3) return "Strong bias toward life safety behavior.";
 746:     if (score >= 1) return "Moderate lean toward life safety.";
 747:     if (score <= -3) return "Strong bias toward security retention.";
 748:     if (score <= -1) return "Moderate lean toward security.";
 749:     return "Balanced conditions — requires design judgment.";
 750:   }
 751: 
 752:   function labelFromSelect(selectEl) {
 753:     if (!selectEl) return "";
 754:     return selectEl.options[selectEl.selectedIndex]?.textContent?.trim() || selectEl.value || "";
 755:   }
 756: 
 757:   function buildInterpretation(recommendation) {
 758:     if (recommendation === "FAIL-SAFE") {
 759:       return "This door leans toward fail-safe behavior because egress reliability and release behavior matter more than retaining the secured state through power loss. That is especially true when the door type or fire/alarm conditions increase life-safety sensitivity.";
 760:     }
 761: 
 762:     if (recommendation === "FAIL-SECURE") {
 763:       return "This door leans toward fail-secure behavior because the security consequence of releasing during outage is higher than the benefit of automatic unlock. That usually happens on perimeter or critical doors where threat pressure and asset protection outweigh convenience.";
 764:     }
 765: 
 766:     return "The door conditions are balanced enough that neither fail-safe nor fail-secure wins cleanly on logic alone. This is where code requirements, occupancy, emergency egress, and actual operational use should drive the final hardware choice.";
 767:   }
 768: 
 769:   function buildGuidance(recommendation) {
 770:     if (recommendation === "FAIL-SAFE") {
 771:       return "Confirm that the lock hardware, release path, and fire-alarm behavior all support safe egress under loss-of-power conditions before moving into reader and power design.";
 772:     }
 773: 
 774:     if (recommendation === "FAIL-SECURE") {
 775:       return "Verify egress method and code treatment carefully. A fail-secure choice is only acceptable if safe exit remains intact under the door’s actual use case and authority requirements.";
 776:     }
 777: 
 778:     return "Do not finalize lock type yet. Escalate this door for code review and operational review before choosing reader placement or power assumptions.";
 779:   }
 780: 
 781:   function getStatusForRecommendation(recommendation, confidence) {
 782:     if (recommendation === "CONDITIONAL") return "WATCH";
 783:     if (confidence === "LOW") return "WATCH";
 784:     return "HEALTHY";
 785:   }
 786: 
 787:   function calculate() {
 788:     const doorType = els.doorType.value;
 789:     const life = els.life.value;
 790:     const powerLoss = els.powerLoss.value;
 791:     const fire = els.fire.value;
 792:     const threat = els.threat.value;
 793: 
 794:     let score = 0;
 795: 
 796:     if (doorType === "stairwell") score += 3;
 797:     if (doorType === "interior") score += 1;
 798:     if (doorType === "perimeter") score -= 1;
 799:     if (doorType === "it") score -= 3;
 800: 
 801:     if (life === "high") score += 3;
 802:     if (life === "med") score += 1;
 803:     if (life === "low") score -= 2;
 804: 
 805:     if (powerLoss === "frequent") score += 2;
 806:     if (powerLoss === "rare") score -= 1;
 807: 
 808:     if (fire === "yes") score += 1;
 809: 
 810:     if (threat === "high") score -= 3;
 811:     if (threat === "med") score -= 1;
 812: 
 813:     let recommendation;
 814:     let rationale;
 815:     let risk;
 816: 
 817:     if (score >= 2) {
 818:       recommendation = "FAIL-SAFE";
 819:       rationale = "Life safety and egress reliability outweigh the need to stay locked during power loss.";
 820:       risk = "Exposure during outage or release conditions.";
 821:     } else if (score <= -2) {
 822:       recommendation = "FAIL-SECURE";
 823:       rationale = "Security retention outweighs automatic release behavior.";
 824:       risk = "Improper egress if not designed correctly.";
 825:     } else {
 826:       recommendation = "CONDITIONAL";
 827:       rationale = "Balanced inputs require code-driven and operational decision.";
 828:       risk = "Inconsistent behavior across doors.";
 829:     }
 830: 
 831:     const confidence = getConfidence(score);
 832:     const scoreMeaning = getScoreMeaning(score);
 833:     const interpretation = buildInterpretation(recommendation);
 834:     const guidance = buildGuidance(recommendation);
 835:     const status = getStatusForRecommendation(recommendation, confidence);
 836: 
 837:     render([
 838:       { label: "Recommendation", value: recommendation },
 839:       { label: "Confidence", value: confidence },
 840:       { label: "Why", value: rationale },
 841:       { label: "Score Meaning", value: scoreMeaning },
 842:       { label: "Primary Risk", value: risk },
 843:       { label: "Score", value: String(score) },
 844:       { label: "Engineering Interpretation", value: interpretation },
 845:       { label: "Actionable Guidance", value: guidance }
 846:     ]);
 847: 
 848:     savePipelineResult({
 849:       recommendation,
 850:       score,
 851:       confidence,
 852:       doorType,
 853:       life,
 854:       powerLoss,
 855:       fire,
 856:       threat
 857:     });
 858: 
 859:     showContinue();
 860: 
 861:     currentReport = buildReportPayload({
 862:       status,
 863:       summary: `${recommendation} is the current planning recommendation with ${confidence.toLowerCase()} confidence. ${rationale}`,
 864:       interpretation,
 865:       inputs: {
 866:         doorTypeLabel: labelFromSelect(els.doorType),
 867:         lifeLabel: labelFromSelect(els.life),
 868:         powerLossLabel: labelFromSelect(els.powerLoss),
 869:         fireLabel: labelFromSelect(els.fire),
 870:         threatLabel: labelFromSelect(els.threat)
 871:       },
 872:       outputs: getRenderedRows()
 873:     });
 874: 
 875:     updateExportControls();
 876:   }
 877: 
 878:   function resetAll() {
 879:     els.doorType.value = "interior";
 880:     els.life.value = "high";
 881:     els.powerLoss.value = "normal";
 882:     els.fire.value = "yes";
 883:     els.threat.value = "low";
 884: 
 885:     currentReport = null;
 886:     invalidatePipelineResult();
 887:     clearResults("Run the evaluation to see results.");
 888:     updateExportControls();
 889:   }
 890: 
 891:   function bindEvents() {
 892:     if (els.calc) {
 893:       els.calc.addEventListener("click", calculate);
 894:     }
 895: 
 896:     if (els.reset) {
 897:       els.reset.addEventListener("click", resetAll);
 898:     }
 899: 
 900:     [
 901:       els.doorType,
 902:       els.life,
 903:       els.powerLoss,
 904:       els.fire,
 905:       els.threat
 906:     ].forEach((el) => {
 907:       if (!el) return;
 908:       el.addEventListener("change", invalidate);
 909:       el.addEventListener("input", invalidate);
 910:     });
 911: 
 912:     if (els.continueBtn) {
 913:       els.continueBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
 914:         window.location.href = "/tools/access-control/reader-type-selector/";
 915:       });
 916:     }
 917: 
 918:     [
 919:       els.reportTitle,
 920:       els.projectName,
 921:       els.clientName,
 922:       els.preparedBy,
 923:       els.customNotes
 924:     ].forEach((el) => {
 925:       if (!el) return;
 926:       el.addEventListener("input", () => {
 927:         if (!currentReport) return;
 928:         updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
 929:       });
 930:     });
 931:   }
 932: 
 933:   function init() {
 934:     const year = document.querySelector("[data-year]");
 935:     if (year) year.textContent = new Date().getFullYear();
 936: 
 937:     resetAll();
 938: 
 939:     setTimeout(() => {
 940:       updateExportControls();
 941:     }, 500);
 942: 
 943:     setTimeout(() => {
 944:       updateExportControls();
 945:     }, 1200);
 946:   }
 947: 
 948:   bindEvents();
 949:   init();
 950: })();
