  52:   };
  53: 
  54:   function normalizeSlug(value) {
  55:     return String(value ?? "").trim().toLowerCase();
  56:   }
  57: 
  58:   function escapeHtml(value) {
  59:     return String(value ?? "")
  60:       .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
  61:       .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
  62:       .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
  63:       .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
  64:       .replace(/'/g, "&#39;");
  65:   }
  66: 
  67:   function formatDateTime(isoString) {
  68:     try {
  69:       return new Date(isoString).toLocaleString();
  70:     } catch {
  71:       return String(isoString || "");
  72:     }
  73:   }
  74: 
  75:   function makeReportId(prefix = "SL-REPORT") {
  76:     const stamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[-:TZ.]/g, "").slice(0, 14);
  77:     return `${prefix}-${stamp}`;
  78:   }

 983:   function loadFlowContext() {
 984:     if (!els.flowNote) return;
 985: 
 986:     const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(FLOW_KEYS[PREVIOUS_STEP]);
 987: 
 988:     if (!raw) {
 989:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
 990:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
 991:       return;
 992:     }
 993: 
 994:     let parsed = null;
 995: 
 996:     try {
 997:       parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
 998:     } catch {
 999:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
1000:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
1001:       return;
1002:     }
1003: 
1004:     if (!parsed || parsed.category !== CATEGORY || parsed.step !== PREVIOUS_STEP) {
1005:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
1006:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
1007:       return;
1008:     }
1009: 
1010:     const d = parsed.data || {};
1011:     const lines = [];
1012: 
1013:     if (d.readerType) lines.push(`Reader Type: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.readerType)}</strong>`);
1014:     if (d.interfaceRec) lines.push(`Interface: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.interfaceRec)}</strong>`);
1015:     if (d.security) lines.push(`Security: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.security)}</strong>`);
1016:     if (d.environment) lines.push(`Environment: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.environment)}</strong>`);
1017:     if (d.credential) lines.push(`Credential: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.credential)}</strong>`);
1018: 
1019:     if (!lines.length) {
1020:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
1021:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
1022:       return;
1023:     }
1024: 
1025:     els.flowNote.hidden = false;
1026:     els.flowNote.innerHTML = `
1027:       <strong>Flow Context</strong><br>
1028:       ${lines.join(" | ")}
1029:       <br><br>
1030:       Use that reader decision as the basis for estimating whether the chosen lock hardware can be supported cleanly under simultaneous unlock demand.
1031:     `;
1032:   }
1033: 
1034:   function collectVisibleResults() {
1035:     if (!els.results) return [];
1036: 
1037:     const rows = Array.from(els.results.querySelectorAll(".result-row"));
1038: 
1039:     return rows.map((rowEl) => {
1040:       const label = rowEl.querySelector(".result-label")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
1041:       const value = rowEl.querySelector(".result-value")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
1042:       return { label, value };
1043:     }).filter((item) => item.label && item.value);
1044:   }
1045: 
1046:   function getSummaryFromResults(outputs) {
1047:     const supply = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Required Supply")?.value || "";
1048:     const watts = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Power")?.value || "";
1049:     const status = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "System Status")?.value || "";
1050: 
1051:     return `Estimated required supply is ${supply || "N/A"} with ${watts || "N/A"} total power and an overall status of ${status || "unknown"}.`;
1052:   }
1053: 
1054:   function getInterpretationFromResults(outputs) {
1055:     return outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Engineering Insight")?.value || "";
1056:   }
1057: 
1058:   function getStatusFromResults(outputs) {
1059:     const status = (outputs.find((x) => x.label === "System Status")?.value || "").toUpperCase();
1060: 
1061:     if (status === "RISK") return "RISK";
1062:     if (status === "WATCH") return "WATCH";
1063:     return "HEALTHY";
1064:   }
1065: 
1066:   function getAssumptions() {
1067:     return [
1068:       "Peak unlock demand is based on simultaneous unlock events, not all installed locks unlocking at once unless configured that way.",
1069:       "Required supply includes the configured design headroom percentage.",
1070:       "This export reflects the current on-screen tool results at the time the report was opened or saved.",
1071:       "Final power design should be checked against manufacturer surge current, hold current, power supply listing, wiring distance, voltage drop, and fire/life-safety behavior."
1072:     ];
1073:   }
1074: 
1075:   function buildCurrentReportPayload() {
1076:     const outputs = collectVisibleResults();
1077: 
1078:     if (!outputs.length) return null;
1079: 
1080:     return {
1081:       reportId: makeReportId("SL-ACC-LOCKPOWER"),
1082:       generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
1083:       category: CATEGORY_LABEL,
1084:       categorySlug: CATEGORY,
1085:       tool: TOOL_LABEL,
1086:       toolSlug: STEP,
1087:       status: getStatusFromResults(outputs),
1088:       summary: getSummaryFromResults(outputs),
1089:       interpretation: getInterpretationFromResults(outputs),
1090:       inputs: [
1091:         { label: "Lock Type", value: els.lockType.options[els.lockType.selectedIndex]?.text || els.lockType.value },
1092:         { label: "Voltage", value: els.voltage.options[els.voltage.selectedIndex]?.text || els.voltage.value },
1093:         { label: "Current per Lock (A)", value: String(els.amps.value) },
1094:         { label: "Number of Locks", value: String(els.locks.value) },
1095:         { label: "Simultaneous Unlocks", value: String(els.simul.value) },
1096:         { label: "Headroom (%)", value: String(els.headroom.value) }
1097:       ],
1098:       outputs,
1099:       assumptions: getAssumptions(),
1100:       chartImage: getExportChartImage(),
1101:       meta: getReportMeta()
1102:     };
1103:   }

1105:   function clearAnalysis() {
1106:     if (window.ScopedLabsAnalyzer && els.analysis) {
1107:       ScopedLabsAnalyzer.clearAnalysisBlock(els.analysis);
1108:     } else if (els.analysis) {
1109:       els.analysis.innerHTML = "";
1110:       els.analysis.style.display = "none";
1111:     }
1112:   }
1113: 
1114:   function invalidate(message = "Run calculation.") {
1115:     try {
1116:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS[STEP]);
1117:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["panel-capacity"]);
1118:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["access-level-sizing"]);
1119:     } catch {}
1120: 
1121:     destroyChart();
1122:     hideContinue();
1123:     clearAnalysis();
1124: 
1125:     if (els.results) {
1126:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>`;
1127:     }
1128: 
1129:     lastMetrics = null;
1130:     currentReport = null;
1131:     updateExportControls();
1132:     loadFlowContext();
1133:   }
1134: 
1135:   function reset() {
1136:     if (els.lockType) els.lockType.value = "strike";
1137:     if (els.voltage) els.voltage.value = "12";
1138:     if (els.amps) els.amps.value = "0.35";
1139:     if (els.locks) els.locks.value = "8";
1140:     if (els.simul) els.simul.value = "2";
1141:     if (els.headroom) els.headroom.value = "25";

1144:   }

1146:   function getStatus(utilizationPct) {
1147:     if (utilizationPct > 85) return "RISK";
1148:     if (utilizationPct > 65) return "WATCH";
1149:     return "HEALTHY";
1150:   }
1151: 
1152:   function getGuidance(status, simul, locks, lockType) {
1153:     if (status === "RISK") {
1154:       return `Power supply margin is too tight. High simultaneous ${lockType} events may cause voltage sag, unlock instability, or nuisance behavior under field conditions.`;
1155:     }
1156: 
1157:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1158:       return `System is serviceable but tight. ${simul} simultaneous unlocks across ${locks} locks leaves limited margin for expansion, cable loss, or supply aging.`;
1159:     }
1160: 
1161:     return "Power budget is clean. Supply sizing should tolerate normal unlock bursts with reasonable field margin.";
1162:   }
1163: 
1164:   function getInsight(status, peak, required, watts) {
1165:     if (status === "RISK") {
1166:       return `Peak event load of ${peak.toFixed(2)} A is pushing the supply too hard. Required budget rises to ${required.toFixed(2)} A / ${watts.toFixed(1)} W once headroom is included, which is not where you want a lock circuit to live.`;
1167:     }
1168: 
1169:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1170:       return "The design is within range, but only with moderate reserve. Unlock bursts, cable losses, and future changes could move this supply from acceptable to problematic.";
1171:     }
1172: 
1173:     return "The design stays well inside a healthy operating envelope. Peak unlock demand and reserved headroom remain balanced, which is what you want for stable lock behavior.";
1174:   }
1175:

1432:   function calc() {
1433:     const amps = parseFloat(els.amps.value);
1434:     const locks = parseInt(els.locks.value, 10);
1435:     const simul = parseInt(els.simul.value, 10);
1436:     const headroom = parseFloat(els.headroom.value);
1437:     const voltage = parseInt(els.voltage.value, 10);
1438: 
1439:     if (
1440:       !Number.isFinite(amps) || amps <= 0 ||
1441:       !Number.isFinite(locks) || locks <= 0 ||
1442:       !Number.isFinite(simul) || simul <= 0 ||
1443:       !Number.isFinite(headroom) || headroom < 0 ||
1444:       !Number.isFinite(voltage) || voltage <= 0
1445:     ) {
1446:       render([row("Error", "Enter valid values for all inputs.")]);
1447:       destroyChart();
1448:       hideContinue();
1449:       lastMetrics = null;
1450:       currentReport = null;
1451:       updateExportControls();
1452:       return;
1453:     }
1454: 
1455:     const effectiveSimul = Math.min(locks, simul);
1456:     const peak = effectiveSimul * amps;
1457:     const required = peak * (1 + headroom / 100);
1458:     const watts = required * voltage;
1459:     const utilizationPct = required > 0 ? (peak / required) * 100 : 0;
1460: 
1461:     const status = getStatus(utilizationPct);
1462:     const guidance = getGuidance(status, effectiveSimul, locks, els.lockType.value);
1463:     const insight = getInsight(status, peak, required, watts);
1464: 
1465:     render([
1466:       row("Peak Load", `${peak.toFixed(2)} A`),
1467:       row("Required Supply", `${required.toFixed(2)} A`),
1468:       row("Power", `${watts.toFixed(1)} W`),
1469:       row("Utilization", `${utilizationPct.toFixed(0)}%`),
1470:       row("System Status", status),
1471:       row("Design Guidance", guidance),
1472:       row("Engineering Insight", insight)
1473:     ]);
1474: 
1475:     lastMetrics = {
1476:       peak,
1477:       required,
1478:       watts,
1479:       utilizationPct
1480:     };
1481: 
1482:     renderChart(lastMetrics);
1483: 
1484:     if (window.ScopedLabsAnalyzer) {
1485:       ScopedLabsAnalyzer.writeFlow(FLOW_KEYS[STEP], {
1486:         category: CATEGORY,
1487:         step: STEP,
1488:         lane: LANE,
1489:         data: {
1490:           peakLoadA: peak,
1491:           requiredSupplyA: required,
1492:           watts,
1493:           utilizationPct,
1494:           status
1495:         }
1496:       });
1497:     }
1498: 
1499:     currentReport = buildCurrentReportPayload();
1500:     updateExportControls();
1501:     showContinue();
1502:   }
1503: 
1504:   function bindEvents() {
1505:     if (els.calc) {
1506:       els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);
1507:     }
1508: 
1509:     if (els.reset) {
1510:       els.reset.addEventListener("click", reset);
1511:     }
1512: 
1513:     [
1514:       els.lockType,
1515:       els.voltage,
1516:       els.amps,
1517:       els.locks,
1518:       els.simul,
1519:       els.headroom
1520:     ].forEach((el) => {
1521:       if (!el) return;
1522:       el.addEventListener("input", () => invalidate("Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results."));
1523:       el.addEventListener("change", () => invalidate("Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results."));
1524:     });
1525: 
1526:     [
1527:       els.reportTitle,
1528:       els.projectName,
1529:       els.clientName,
1530:       els.preparedBy,
1531:       els.customNotes
1532:     ].forEach((el) => {
1533:       if (!el) return;
1534:       el.addEventListener("input", () => {
1535:         if (!currentReport) return;
1536:         updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
1537:       });
1538:     });
1539: 
1540:     if (els.nextBtn) {
1541:       els.nextBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
1542:         window.location.href = "/tools/access-control/panel-capacity/";
1543:       });
1544:     }
1545:   }
1546: 
1547:   function init() {
1548:     const year = document.querySelector("[data-year]");
1549:     if (year) year.textContent = new Date().getFullYear();
1550: 
1551:     reset();
1552: 
1553:     unlockCategoryPage();
1554: 
1555:     setTimeout(() => {
1556:       unlockCategoryPage();
1557:       updateExportControls();
1558:     }, 400);
1559: 
1560:     setTimeout(() => {
1561:       unlockCategoryPage();
1562:       updateExportControls();
1563:     }, 1200);
1564:   }
1565:

1567:   init();
1568: })();

 328:   function readSnapshots(key) {
 329:     try {
 330:       const raw = localStorage.getItem(key);
 331:       const parsed = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : [];
 332:       return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
 333:     } catch {
 334:       return [];
 335:     }
 336:   }
 337: 
 338:   function writeSnapshots(key, items) {
 339:     localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items));
 340:   }
 341: 
 342:   function saveSnapshotToStorage(key, payload, limit = 25) {
 343:     const existing = readSnapshots(key);
 344: 
 345:     existing.unshift({
 346:       ...payload,
 347:       savedAt: new Date().toISOString()
 348:     });
 349: 
 350:     const trimmed = existing.slice(0, limit);
 351:     writeSnapshots(key, trimmed);
 352: 
 353:     return trimmed.length;
 354:   }

 462:           ctx.strokeStyle = "#198754";
 463:           ctx.lineWidth = 3;
 464:           ctx.setLineDash([6, 5]);
 465:           ctx.beginPath();
 466:           ctx.moveTo(rx, top);
 467:           ctx.lineTo(rx, bottom);
 468:           ctx.stroke();
 469:           ctx.setLineDash([]);
 470: 
 471:           ctx.fillStyle = "#1f2937";
 472:           ctx.font = "600 16px Arial";
 473:           ctx.fillText("Healthy Capacity Floor", rx + 10, bottom - 12);
 474: 
 475:           ctx.fillStyle = "#15803d";
 476:           ctx.font = "700 15px Arial";
 477:           ctx.fillText("Healthy", x.getPixelForValue(6), top + 18);
 478: 
 479:           ctx.fillStyle = "#b45309";
 480:           ctx.fillText("Watch", x.getPixelForValue(69), top + 18);
 481: 
 482:           ctx.fillStyle = "#b91c1c";
 483:           ctx.fillText("Risk", x.getPixelForValue(89), top + 18);
 484: 
 485:           const dominantValue = values[dominantIndex];
 486:           const px = x.getPixelForValue(dominantValue);
 487:           const py = y.getPixelForValue(labels[dominantIndex]);
 488: 
 489:           ctx.beginPath();
 490:           ctx.arc(px, py, 6, 0, Math.PI * 2);
 491:           ctx.fillStyle = "#ffffff";
 492:           ctx.fill();
 493:           ctx.strokeStyle = "#111827";
 494:           ctx.lineWidth = 2;
 495:           ctx.stroke();
 496: 
 497:           ctx.fillStyle = "#1f2937";
 498:           ctx.font = "600 15px Arial";
 499:           ctx.fillText(displayValues[dominantIndex], Math.min(px + 10, chartArea.right - 120), py - 10);
 500: 
 501:           ctx.restore();
 502:         }
 503:       };
 504: 
 505:       exportChart = new Chart(ctx, {
 506:         type: "bar",
 507:         data: {
 508:           labels,
 509:           datasets: [
 510:             {
 511:               label: "Panel Capacity Metrics",
 512:               data: values,
 513:               indexAxis: "y",
 514:               barThickness: 18,
 515:               maxBarThickness: 18,
 516:               barPercentage: 0.8,
 517:               categoryPercentage: 0.7,
 518:               borderRadius: 8,
 519:               borderSkipped: false,
 520:               borderWidth: 1.5,
 521:               backgroundColor: (context) => {
 522:                 const i = context.dataIndex;
 523:                 const v = context.raw;
 524: 
 525:                 if (i === dominantIndex) {
 526:                   if (v > 85) return "#dc2626";
 527:                   if (v > 65) return "#f59e0b";
 528:                   return "#22c55e";
 529:                 }
 530: 
 531:                 if (v > 85) return "rgba(220, 38, 38, 0.55)";
 532:                 if (v > 65) return "rgba(245, 158, 11, 0.50)";
 533:                 return "rgba(59, 130, 246, 0.42)";
 534:               },
 535:               borderColor: (context) => {
 536:                 const i = context.dataIndex;
 537:                 const v = context.raw;
 538: 
 539:                 if (i === dominantIndex) {
 540:                   if (v > 85) return "#7f1d1d";
 541:                   if (v > 65) return "#92400e";
 542:                   return "#166534";
 543:                 }
 544: 
 545:                 if (v > 85) return "#991b1b";
 546:                 if (v > 65) return "#b45309";
 547:                 return "#1d4ed8";
 548:               }
 549:             }
 550:           ]
 551:         },
 552:         options: {
 553:           responsive: false,
 554:           maintainAspectRatio: false,
 555:           animation: false,
 556:           indexAxis: "y",
 557:           layout: {
 558:             padding: {
 559:               top: 36,
 560:               right: 22,
 561:               bottom: 10,
 562:               left: 18
 563:             }
 564:           },
 565:           plugins: {
 566:             legend: { display: false },
 567:             tooltip: { enabled: false }
 568:           },
 569:           scales: {
 570:             x: {
 571:               beginAtZero: true,
 572:               suggestedMax: Math.ceil(maxValue * 1.08),
 573:               ticks: {
 574:                 color: "#334155",
 575:                 font: {
 576:                   size: 14,
 577:                   weight: "600"
 578:                 }
 579:               },
 580:               grid: {
 581:                 color: "rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.08)"
 582:               },
 583:               border: {
 584:                 color: "rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.18)"
 585:               },
 586:               title: {
 587:                 display: true,
 588:                 text: "Capacity Stress Magnitude",
 589:                 color: "#0f172a",
 590:                 font: {
 591:                   size: 15,
 592:                   weight: "700"
 593:                 }
 594:               }
 595:             },
 596:             y: {
 597:               ticks: {
 598:                 color: "#0f172a",
 599:                 font: {
 600:                   size: 15,
 601:                   weight: "700"
 602:                 }
 603:               },
 604:               grid: {
 605:                 display: false
 606:               },
 607:               border: {
 608:                 color: "rgba(15, 23, 42, 0.18)"
 609:               }
 610:             }
 611:           }
 612:         },
 613:         plugins: [bgPlugin]
 614:       });
 615: 
 616:       const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL("image/png", 1);
 617: 
 618:       if (exportChart) {
 619:         exportChart.destroy();
 620:         exportChart = null;
 621:       }
 622: 
 623:       return dataUrl;
 624:     } catch (err) {
 625:       console.error("Export chart render failed:", err);
 626:       return getChartImage();
 627:     }
 628:   }

 972:   function openReportWindow(payload) {
 973:     try {
 974:       const html = buildReportHTML(payload);
 975:       const blob = new Blob([html], { type: "text/html" });
 976:       const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
 977:       const win = window.open(url, "_blank");
 978: 
 979:       if (!win) return false;
 980: 
 981:       setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(url), 10000);
 982:       return true;
 983:     } catch (err) {
 984:       console.error("Export report open failed:", err);
 985:       return false;
 986:     }
 987:   }
 988: 
 989:   function loadFlowContext() {
 990:     if (!els.flowNote) return;
 991: 
 992:     const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(FLOW_KEYS[PREVIOUS_STEP]);
 993: 
 994:     if (!raw) {
 995:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
 996:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
 997:       return;
 998:     }
 999: 
1000:     let parsed = null;
1001: 
1002:     try {
1003:       parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
1004:     } catch {
1005:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
1006:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
1007:       return;
1008:     }
1009: 
1010:     if (!parsed || parsed.category !== CATEGORY || parsed.step !== PREVIOUS_STEP) {
1011:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
1012:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
1013:       return;
1014:     }
1015: 
1016:     const d = parsed.data || {};
1017:     const lines = [];
1018: 
1019:     if (Number.isFinite(Number(d.peakLoadA))) lines.push(`Peak Load: <strong>${Number(d.peakLoadA).toFixed(2)} A</strong>`);
1020:     if (Number.isFinite(Number(d.requiredSupplyA))) lines.push(`Required Supply: <strong>${Number(d.requiredSupplyA).toFixed(2)} A</strong>`);
1021:     if (Number.isFinite(Number(d.watts))) lines.push(`Power: <strong>${Number(d.watts).toFixed(1)} W</strong>`);
1022:     if (d.status) lines.push(`Power Status: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.status)}</strong>`);
1023: 
1024:     if (!lines.length) {
1025:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
1026:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
1027:       return;
1028:     }
1029: 
1030:     els.flowNote.hidden = false;
1031:     els.flowNote.innerHTML = `
1032:       <strong>Flow Context</strong><br>
1033:       ${lines.join(" | ")}
1034:       <br><br>
1035:       Use that lock-power result as the basis for deciding how much controller and expansion capacity the full system really needs with growth margin included.
1036:     `;
1037:   }
1038: 
1039:   function collectVisibleResults() {
1040:     if (!els.results) return [];
1041: 
1042:     return Array.from(els.results.querySelectorAll(".result-row"))
1043:       .map((rowEl) => {
1044:         const label = rowEl.querySelector(".result-label")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
1045:         const value = rowEl.querySelector(".result-value")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
1046:         return { label, value };
1047:       })
1048:       .filter((item) => item.label && item.value);
1049:   }
1050: 
1051:   function getSummaryFromResults(outputs) {
1052:     const panels = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Panels Required")?.value || "";
1053:     const expansions = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Expansion Modules")?.value || "";
1054:     const status = outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Status")?.value || "";
1055: 
1056:     return `Estimated architecture requires ${panels || "N/A"} panels with ${expansions || "N/A"} expansion modules and an overall status of ${status || "unknown"}.`;
1057:   }
1058: 
1059:   function getInterpretationFromResults(outputs) {
1060:     return outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Engineering Insight")?.value || "";
1061:   }
1062: 
1063:   function getStatusFromResults(outputs) {
1064:     const status = (outputs.find((x) => x.label === "Status")?.value || "").toUpperCase();
1065: 
1066:     if (status === "RISK") return "RISK";
1067:     if (status === "WATCH") return "WATCH";
1068:     return "HEALTHY";
1069:   }
1070: 
1071:   function getAssumptions() {
1072:     return [
1073:       "Panel requirement is based on target doors including spare capacity, then compared against base and expansion door capacity.",
1074:       "Reader totals, input totals, and output totals are planning references and should be validated against the selected controller platform.",
1075:       "This export reflects the current on-screen tool results at the time the report was opened or saved.",
1076:       "Final architecture should be verified against manufacturer capacity, licensing, IO limits, expansion rules, wiring topology, and owner growth expectations."
1077:     ];
1078:   }
1079: 
1080:   function buildCurrentReportPayload() {
1081:     const outputs = collectVisibleResults();
1082: 
1083:     if (!outputs.length) return null;
1084: 
1085:     return {
1086:       reportId: makeReportId("SL-ACC-PANEL"),
1087:       generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
1088:       category: CATEGORY_LABEL,
1089:       categorySlug: CATEGORY,
1090:       tool: TOOL_LABEL,
1091:       toolSlug: STEP,
1092:       status: getStatusFromResults(outputs),
1093:       summary: getSummaryFromResults(outputs),
1094:       interpretation: getInterpretationFromResults(outputs),
1095:       inputs: [
1096:         { label: "Doors", value: String(els.doors.value) },
1097:         { label: "Readers per Door", value: els.readersPerDoor.options[els.readersPerDoor.selectedIndex]?.text || els.readersPerDoor.value },
1098:         { label: "Inputs per Door", value: String(els.inputsPerDoor.value) },
1099:         { label: "Outputs per Door", value: String(els.outputsPerDoor.value) },

1154:   function getStatus(loadPct) {
1155:     if (loadPct > 85) return "RISK";
1156:     if (loadPct > 65) return "WATCH";
1157:     return "HEALTHY";

1160:   function getInsight(status) {
1161:     if (status === "RISK") {
1162:       return "Panel architecture is too dense. Expansion paths are near exhaustion, which increases upgrade cost and reduces flexibility for growth.";
1163:     }
1164: 
1165:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1166:       return "System is serviceable but nearing expansion limits. Plan for additional panels or segmentation before future adds consume remaining capacity.";
1167:     }
1168: 
1169:     return "Panel architecture is balanced with solid remaining growth margin and manageable expansion pressure.";
1170:   }
1171: 
1172:   function getGuidance(status) {
1173:     if (status === "RISK") {
1174:       return "Add controller capacity or split the system into additional panel groups before deployment. Do not build a new system at this density unless there is a clear expansion plan.";
1175:     }
1176: 
1177:     if (status === "WATCH") {
1178:       return "Design is workable, but future expansion should be planned now. Leave physical space, pathway capacity, and licensing room for the next growth phase.";
1179:     }
1180: 
1181:     return "Architecture is healthy. Existing panel and expansion assumptions leave practical room for growth and normal field changes.";
1182:   }

1213:     const referenceValue = 65;
1214:     const chartMax = Math.max(100, Math.ceil(Math.max(...values, referenceValue, 85) * 1.12));
1215: 
1216:     const chartBgPlugin = {
1217:       id: "chartBgPlugin",
1218:       beforeDraw(c) {
1219:         const { ctx, chartArea } = c;
1220:         if (!chartArea) return;

1222:         const { left, top, width, height } = chartArea;
1223: 
1224:         ctx.save();
1225:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255,255,255,0.05)";
1226:         ctx.fillRect(left, top, width, height);
1227:         ctx.restore();
1228:       }
1229:     };
1230: 
1231:     const thresholdBandPlugin = {
1232:       id: "thresholdBandPlugin",
1233:       beforeDatasetsDraw(c) {
1234:         const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = c;
1235:         if (!chartArea || !scales.x) return;
1236: 
1237:         const x = scales.x;
1238:         const { top, bottom, left, right } = chartArea;
1239: 
1240:         const healthyMax = Math.min(65, x.max);
1241:         const watchMax = Math.min(85, x.max);
1242: 
1243:         ctx.save();
1244: 
1245:         if (healthyMax > 0) {
1246:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(46, 204, 113, 0.16)";
1247:           ctx.fillRect(left, top, x.getPixelForValue(healthyMax) - left, bottom - top);
1248:         }
1249: 
1250:         if (watchMax > 65) {
1251:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 200, 80, 0.13)";
1252:           ctx.fillRect(
1253:             x.getPixelForValue(65),
1254:             top,
1255:             x.getPixelForValue(watchMax) - x.getPixelForValue(65),
1256:             bottom - top
1257:           );
1258:         }
1259: 
1260:         if (x.max > 85) {
1261:           ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 90, 90, 0.13)";
1262:           ctx.fillRect(
1263:             x.getPixelForValue(85),
1264:             top,
1265:             right - x.getPixelForValue(85),
1266:             bottom - top
1267:           );
1268:         }
1269: 
1270:         ctx.restore();
1271:       },
1272:       afterDatasetsDraw(c) {
1273:         const { ctx, chartArea, scales } = c;
1274:         if (!chartArea || !scales.x || !scales.y) return;
1275: 
1276:         const x = scales.x;
1277:         const y = scales.y;
1278:         const { top, bottom } = chartArea;
1279: 
1280:         ctx.save();
1281: 
1282:         const rx = x.getPixelForValue(referenceValue);
1283:         ctx.strokeStyle = "rgba(120, 255, 170, 0.98)";
1284:         ctx.lineWidth = 3;
1285:         ctx.setLineDash([4, 4]);
1286:         ctx.beginPath();
1287:         ctx.moveTo(rx, top);
1288:         ctx.lineTo(rx, bottom);
1289:         ctx.stroke();
1290:         ctx.setLineDash([]);
1291: 
1292:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(220, 255, 235, 0.96)";
1293:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1294:         ctx.fillText("Healthy Capacity Floor", rx + 8, bottom - 10);
1295: 
1296:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(180, 255, 200, 0.82)";
1297:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1298:         ctx.fillText("Healthy", x.getPixelForValue(6), top + 14);
1299: 
1300:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 220, 140, 0.82)";
1301:         ctx.fillText("Watch", x.getPixelForValue(69), top + 14);
1302: 
1303:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(255, 160, 160, 0.82)";
1304:         ctx.fillText("Risk", x.getPixelForValue(89), top + 14);
1305: 
1306:         const dominantValue = values[dominantIndex];
1307:         const px = x.getPixelForValue(dominantValue);
1308:         const py = y.getPixelForValue(labels[dominantIndex]);
1309: 
1310:         ctx.beginPath();
1311:         ctx.arc(px, py, 4.5, 0, Math.PI * 2);
1312:         ctx.fillStyle = "rgba(225, 255, 240, 1)";
1313:         ctx.fill();
1314:         ctx.strokeStyle = "rgba(120, 255, 170, 0.95)";
1315:         ctx.lineWidth = 2;
1316:         ctx.stroke();
1317:

1319:         ctx.font = "600 11px sans-serif";
1320:         ctx.fillText(displayValues[dominantIndex], Math.min(px + 8, chartArea.right - 110), py - 8);
1321: 
1322:         ctx.restore();
1323:       }
1324:     };
1325: 
1326:     chart = new Chart(els.chart, {
1327:       type: "bar",

1440:   function calc() {
1441:     const doors = numberValue(els.doors);
1442:     const readersPerDoor = numberValue(els.readersPerDoor);
1443:     const inputsPerDoor = numberValue(els.inputsPerDoor);
1444:     const outputsPerDoor = numberValue(els.outputsPerDoor);
1445:     const spare = numberValue(els.spare);
1446:     const base = numberValue(els.baseDoors);
1447:     const exp = numberValue(els.expDoors);
1448:     const maxExp = numberValue(els.maxExp);
1449: 
1450:     if (
1451:       !Number.isFinite(doors) || doors <= 0 ||
1452:       !Number.isFinite(readersPerDoor) || readersPerDoor <= 0 ||
1453:       !Number.isFinite(inputsPerDoor) || inputsPerDoor < 0 ||
1454:       !Number.isFinite(outputsPerDoor) || outputsPerDoor < 0 ||
1455:       !Number.isFinite(spare) || spare < 0 ||
1456:       !Number.isFinite(base) || base <= 0 ||
1457:       !Number.isFinite(exp) || exp <= 0 ||
1458:       !Number.isFinite(maxExp) || maxExp <= 0
1459:     ) {
1460:       render([row("Error", "Enter valid values for all inputs.")]);
1461:       destroyChart();
1462:       hideContinue();
1463:       lastMetrics = null;
1464:       currentReport = null;
1465:       updateExportControls();
1466:       return;
1467:     }
1468: 
1469:     const targetDoors = Math.ceil(doors * (1 + spare / 100));
1470:     const perPanelCapacity = base + (maxExp * exp);
1471:     const panels = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(targetDoors / perPanelCapacity));
1472: 
1473:     const baseCapacityTotal = panels * base;
1474:     const remainingAfterBase = Math.max(0, targetDoors - baseCapacityTotal);
1475:     const expansions = Math.min(panels * maxExp, Math.ceil(remainingAfterBase / exp));
1476: 
1477:     const panelCapacity = panels * perPanelCapacity;
1478:     const spareDoors = Math.max(0, panelCapacity - doors);
1479:     const readers = Math.ceil(doors * readersPerDoor);
1480:     const totalInputs = Math.ceil(doors * inputsPerDoor);
1481:     const totalOutputs = Math.ceil(doors * outputsPerDoor);
1482: 
1483:     const loadPct = (targetDoors / panelCapacity) * 100;
1484:     const expansionPct = panels > 0 && maxExp > 0 ? (expansions / (panels * maxExp)) * 100 : 0;
1485: 
1486:     const status = getStatus(loadPct);
1487:     const insight = getInsight(status);
1488:     const guidance = getGuidance(status);
1489: 
1490:     render([
1491:       row("Panels Required", panels),
1492:       row("Expansion Modules", expansions),
1493:       row("Panel Door Capacity", panelCapacity),
1494:       row("Target Doors with Spare", targetDoors),
1495:       row("Spare Door Capacity", spareDoors),
1496:       row("Total Readers", readers),
1497:       row("Total Inputs", totalInputs),
1498:       row("Total Outputs", totalOutputs),
1499:       row("System Load", `${loadPct.toFixed(0)}%`),
1500:       row("Expansion Pressure", `${expansionPct.toFixed(0)}%`),
1501:       row("Status", status),
1502:       row("Design Guidance", guidance),
1503:       row("Engineering Insight", insight)
1504:     ]);
1505: 
1506:     lastMetrics = {
1507:       loadPct,
1508:       expansionPct,
1509:       panels,
1510:       readers
1511:     };
1512: 
1513:     renderChart(lastMetrics);
1514: 
1515:     if (window.ScopedLabsAnalyzer) {
1516:       ScopedLabsAnalyzer.writeFlow(FLOW_KEYS[STEP], {
1517:         category: CATEGORY,
1518:         step: STEP,
1519:         lane: LANE,
1520:         data: {
1521:           panels,
1522:           expansions,
1523:           readers,
1524:           totalInputs,
1525:           totalOutputs,
1526:           panelCapacity,
1527:           targetDoors,
1528:           spareDoors,
1529:           loadPct,
1530:           expansionPct,
1531:           utilizationPct: loadPct,
1532:           status
1533:         }
1534:       });
1535:     }
1536: 
1537:     currentReport = buildCurrentReportPayload();
1538:     updateExportControls();
1539:     showContinue();
1540:   }
1541: 
1542:   function bindEvents() {
1543:     if (els.calc) {
1544:       els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);
1545:     }
1546: 
1547:     if (els.reset) {
1548:       els.reset.addEventListener("click", reset);
1549:     }
1550: 
1551:     [
1552:       els.doors,
1553:       els.readersPerDoor,
1554:       els.inputsPerDoor,
1555:       els.outputsPerDoor,
1556:       els.baseDoors,
1557:       els.expDoors,
1558:       els.maxExp,
1559:       els.spare
1560:     ].forEach((el) => {
1561:       if (!el) return;
1562:       el.addEventListener("input", () => invalidate("Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results."));
1563:       el.addEventListener("change", () => invalidate("Inputs changed. Press Calculate to refresh results."));
1564:     });
1565: 
1566:     [
1567:       els.reportTitle,
1568:       els.projectName,
1569:       els.clientName,
1570:       els.preparedBy,
1571:       els.customNotes
1572:     ].forEach((el) => {
1573:       if (!el) return;
1574:       el.addEventListener("input", () => {
1575:         if (!currentReport) return;
1576:         updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
1577:       });
1578:     });
1579: 
1580:     if (els.nextBtn) {
1581:       els.nextBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
1582:         window.location.href = "/tools/access-control/access-level-sizing/";
1583:       });
1584:     }
1585:   }
1586: 
1587:   function init() {
1588:     const year = document.querySelector("[data-year]");
1589:     if (year) year.textContent = new Date().getFullYear();
1590: 
1591:     reset();
1592: 
1593:     unlockCategoryPage();
1594:

1596:       unlockCategoryPage();
1597:       updateExportControls();
1598:     }, 400);
1599: 
1600:     setTimeout(() => {
1601:       unlockCategoryPage();
1602:       updateExportControls();
1603:     }, 1200);
1604:   }

1606:   bindEvents();
1607:   init();
1608: })();

 220:   }
 221: 
 222:   function updateExportControls(message) {
 223:     const unlocked = hasExportAccess();
 224:     const ready = !!currentReport;
 225: 
 226:     setExportEnabled(unlocked && ready);
 227: 
 228:     if (message !== undefined) {
 229:       setExportStatus(message);
 230:       return;
 231:     }
 232: 
 233:     if (!unlocked) {
 234:       setExportStatus("Export is available with Access Control category unlock.");
 235:       return;
 236:     }
 237: 
 238:     if (!ready) {
 239:       setExportStatus("Run recommendation to enable export.");
 240:       return;
 241:     }
 242: 
 243:     setExportStatus("Recommendation ready. Open Export Report or Save Snapshot.");
 244:   }

 246:   function getReportMeta() {
 247:     return {
 248:       reportTitle: (els.reportTitle?.value || "").trim() || "Reader Type Selector Assessment",
 249:       projectName: (els.projectName?.value || "").trim(),
 250:       clientName: (els.clientName?.value || "").trim(),
 251:       preparedBy: (els.preparedBy?.value || "").trim(),
 252:       customNotes: (els.customNotes?.value || "").trim()
 253:     };
 254:   }

 256:   function assumptionsForTool() {
 257:     return [
 258:       "Reader recommendations are planning guidance and must be verified against the selected access-control platform.",
 259:       "Interface recommendations assume the panel and reader hardware support the selected signaling method.",
 260:       "Outdoor and harsh-environment recommendations should be verified against manufacturer environmental ratings.",
 261:       "Credential and authentication choices should be aligned with site security policy, user workflow, and lifecycle support."
 262:     ];
 263:   }

 265:   function showContinue() {
 266:     if (els.nextWrap) els.nextWrap.style.display = "flex";
 267:     if (els.nextBtn) els.nextBtn.disabled = false;
 268:   }
 269: 
 270:   function hideContinue() {
 271:     if (els.nextWrap) els.nextWrap.style.display = "none";
 272:     if (els.nextBtn) els.nextBtn.disabled = true;
 273:   }

 275:   function clearAnalysis() {
 276:     if (window.ScopedLabsAnalyzer && els.analysis) {
 277:       ScopedLabsAnalyzer.clearAnalysisBlock(els.analysis);
 278:     } else if (els.analysis) {
 279:       els.analysis.innerHTML = "";
 280:       els.analysis.style.display = "none";
 281:     }
 282:   }

 284:   function clearResults(message = "Run recommendation.") {
 285:     if (els.results) {
 286:       els.results.innerHTML = `<div class="muted">${escapeHtml(message)}</div>`;
 287:     }
 288: 
 289:     clearAnalysis();
 290:   }
 291: 
 292:   function render(rows) {
 293:     if (!els.results) return;
 294: 
 295:     els.results.innerHTML = "";
 296: 
 297:     rows.forEach((r) => {
 298:       const div = document.createElement("div");
 299:       div.className = "result-row";
 300:       div.innerHTML = `
 301:         <span class="result-label">${escapeHtml(r.label)}</span>
 302:         <span class="result-value">${escapeHtml(r.value)}</span>
 303:       `;
 304:       els.results.appendChild(div);
 305:     });
 306:   }
 307: 
 308:   function getRenderedRows() {
 309:     if (!els.results) return [];
 310: 
 311:     return Array.from(els.results.querySelectorAll(".result-row"))
 312:       .map((row) => {
 313:         const label = row.querySelector(".result-label")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 314:         const value = row.querySelector(".result-value")?.textContent?.trim() || "";
 315:         return { label, value };
 316:       })
 317:       .filter((item) => item.label || item.value);
 318:   }
 319: 
 320:   function readSnapshots(key) {
 321:     try {
 322:       const raw = localStorage.getItem(key);
 323:       const parsed = raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : [];
 324:       return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];
 325:     } catch {
 326:       return [];
 327:     }
 328:   }
 329: 
 330:   function writeSnapshots(key, items) {
 331:     localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(items));
 332:   }

 710:   function loadFlowContext() {
 711:     const raw = sessionStorage.getItem(FLOW_KEYS[PREVIOUS_STEP]);
 712: 
 713:     if (!raw) {
 714:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
 715:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
 716:       return;
 717:     }
 718: 
 719:     let parsed;
 720: 
 721:     try {
 722:       parsed = JSON.parse(raw);
 723:     } catch {
 724:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
 725:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
 726:       return;
 727:     }
 728: 
 729:     if (!parsed || parsed.category !== CATEGORY || parsed.step !== PREVIOUS_STEP) {
 730:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
 731:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
 732:       return;
 733:     }
 734: 
 735:     const d = parsed.data || {};
 736:     const lines = [];
 737: 
 738:     if (d.recommendation) lines.push(`Fail Mode: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.recommendation)}</strong>`);
 739:     if (d.doorType) lines.push(`Door Type: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.doorType)}</strong>`);
 740:     if (d.life) lines.push(`Life Safety: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.life)}</strong>`);
 741:     if (d.threat) lines.push(`Threat: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.threat)}</strong>`);
 742:     if (d.powerLoss) lines.push(`Power Reliability: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.powerLoss)}</strong>`);
 743:     if (d.fire) lines.push(`Fire Integration: <strong>${escapeHtml(d.fire)}</strong>`);
 744: 
 745:     if (!lines.length) {
 746:       els.flowNote.hidden = true;
 747:       els.flowNote.innerHTML = "";
 748:       return;
 749:     }
 750: 
 751:     els.flowNote.hidden = false;
 752:     els.flowNote.innerHTML = `
 753:       <strong>Flow Context</strong><br>
 754:       ${lines.join(" | ")}
 755:       <br><br>
 756:       Use that door-behavior decision to choose a reader style that fits the security need, environment, and user experience instead of selecting reader hardware in isolation.
 757:     `;
 758:   }
 759: 
 760:   function invalidate() {
 761:     try {
 762:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS[STEP]);
 763:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["lock-power-budget"]);
 764:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["panel-capacity"]);
 765:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["access-level-sizing"]);
 766:     } catch {}
 767: 
 768:     currentReport = null;
 769:     hideContinue();
 770:     clearResults("Inputs changed. Press Recommend to refresh results.");
 771:     loadFlowContext();
 772:     updateExportControls();
 773:   }
 774: 
 775:   function resetAll() {
 776:     if (els.sec) els.sec.value = "low";
 777:     if (els.cred) els.cred.value = "card";
 778:     if (els.env) els.env.value = "indoor";
 779:     if (els.throughput) els.throughput.value = "standard";
 780:     if (els.iface) els.iface.value = "wg";
 781: 
 782:     currentReport = null;
 783: 
 784:     try {
 785:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS[STEP]);
 786:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["lock-power-budget"]);
 787:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["panel-capacity"]);
 788:       sessionStorage.removeItem(FLOW_KEYS["access-level-sizing"]);
 789:     } catch {}
 790: 
 791:     hideContinue();
 792:     clearResults("Run recommendation.");
 793:     loadFlowContext();
 794:     updateExportControls();
 795:   }

 797:   function getStatus({ sec, iface, cred }) {
 798:     if (sec === "high" && iface === "wg") return "WATCH";
 799:     if (sec === "high" && cred !== "multi") return "WATCH";
 800:     return "HEALTHY";
 801:   }
 802: 
 803:   function buildSummary({ reader, interfaceRec, security }) {
 804:     return `${reader} is the current planning recommendation. ${security}. Interface recommendation: ${interfaceRec}.`;
 805:   }
 806: 
 807:   function calc() {
 808:     const sec = els.sec.value;
 809:     const cred = els.cred.value;
 810:     const env = els.env.value;
 811:     const throughput = els.throughput.value;
 812:     const iface = els.iface.value;
 813: 
 814:     const interfaceRec =
 815:       iface === "osdp"
 816:         ? "OSDP (secure, supervised)"
 817:         : "Wiegand (legacy, not encrypted)";
 818: 
 819:     let reader = "Smart card reader";
 820:     if (cred === "mobile") reader = "Mobile credential reader";
 821:     if (cred === "pin") reader = "Keypad reader";
 822:     if (cred === "multi") reader = "Multi-factor reader";
 823: 
 824:     const security =
 825:       sec === "high"
 826:         ? "Encrypted credentials + OSDP + MFA recommended"
 827:         : sec === "med"
 828:           ? "Encrypted credentials recommended"
 829:           : "Standard credentials acceptable";
 830: 
 831:     const envNote =
 832:       env === "harsh"
 833:         ? "Use industrial/IP-rated reader"
 834:         : env === "outdoor"
 835:           ? "Use weather-rated reader"
 836:           : "Indoor-rated reader is fine";
 837: 
 838:     const throughputNote =
 839:       throughput === "handsfree"
 840:         ? "Long-range / BLE readers required"
 841:         : throughput === "fast"
 842:           ? "Optimize for fast authentication"
 843:           : "Standard read speed acceptable";
 844: 
 845:     let interpretation = "";
 846:     if (cred === "multi" || sec === "high") {
 847:       interpretation = "This door is being treated as a higher-assurance checkpoint, so reader choice should prioritize credential integrity and stronger supervision over convenience alone.";
 848:     } else if (throughput === "handsfree") {
 849:       interpretation = "This opening is being optimized for flow and convenience, which changes the reader decision away from standard wall-reader assumptions and toward faster user interaction patterns.";
 850:     } else {
 851:       interpretation = "The recommended reader type is balanced for normal access-control conditions, where security, usability, and environment all matter but none of them are extreme enough to dominate the design outright.";
 852:     }
 853: 
 854:     const guidance =
 855:       iface === "wg"
 856:         ? "If the panel can support it, consider moving away from Wiegand on new deployments so the reader decision does not lock the project into weaker signaling and less supervision."
 857:         : "OSDP is the stronger default here. Keep wiring, reader compatibility, and address planning aligned early so the interface choice stays clean through deployment.";
 858: 
 859:     render([
 860:       { label: "Reader Type", value: reader },
 861:       { label: "Interface", value: interfaceRec },
 862:       { label: "Security", value: security },
 863:       { label: "Environment", value: envNote },
 864:       { label: "Throughput", value: throughputNote },
 865:       { label: "Engineering Interpretation", value: interpretation },
 866:       { label: "Actionable Guidance", value: guidance }
 867:     ]);
 868: 
 869:     ScopedLabsAnalyzer.writeFlow(FLOW_KEYS[STEP], {
 870:       category: CATEGORY,
 871:       step: STEP,
 872:       lane: LANE,
 873:       data: {
 874:         readerType: reader,
 875:         interfaceRec,
 876:         security,
 877:         envNote,
 878:         throughputNote,
 879:         environment: env,
 880:         priority: sec,
 881:         credential: cred,
 882:         interface: iface
 883:       }
 884:     });
 885: 
 886:     showContinue();
 887: 
 888:     currentReport = buildReportPayload({
 889:       status: getStatus({ sec, iface, cred }),
 890:       summary: buildSummary({ reader, interfaceRec, security }),
 891:       interpretation,
 892:       inputs: {
 893:         securityLevel: labelFromSelect(els.sec),
 894:         credentialPreference: labelFromSelect(els.cred),
 895:         environment: labelFromSelect(els.env),
 896:         throughput: labelFromSelect(els.throughput),
 897:         interfaceChoice: labelFromSelect(els.iface)
 898:       },
 899:       outputs: getRenderedRows()
 900:     });
 901: 
 902:     updateExportControls();
 903:   }
 904: 
 905:   function bindEvents() {
 906:     if (els.calc) {
 907:       els.calc.addEventListener("click", calc);
 908:     }
 909: 
 910:     if (els.reset) {
 911:       els.reset.addEventListener("click", resetAll);
 912:     }
 913: 
 914:     [
 915:       els.sec,
 916:       els.cred,
 917:       els.env,
 918:       els.throughput,
 919:       els.iface
 920:     ].forEach((el) => {
 921:       if (!el) return;
 922:       el.addEventListener("input", invalidate);
 923:       el.addEventListener("change", invalidate);
 924:     });
 925: 
 926:     if (els.nextBtn) {
 927:       els.nextBtn.addEventListener("click", () => {
 928:         window.location.href = "/tools/access-control/lock-power-budget/";
 929:       });
 930:     }
 931: 
 932:     [
 933:       els.reportTitle,
 934:       els.projectName,
 935:       els.clientName,
 936:       els.preparedBy,
 937:       els.customNotes
 938:     ].forEach((el) => {
 939:       if (!el) return;
 940:       el.addEventListener("input", () => {
 941:         if (!currentReport) return;
 942:         updateExportControls("Export details updated.");
 943:       });
 944:     });
 945:   }
 946: 
 947:   function init() {
 948:     const year = document.querySelector("[data-year]");
 949:     if (year) year.textContent = new Date().getFullYear();
 950: 
 951:     currentReport = null;
 952:     hideContinue();
 953:     clearResults("Run recommendation.");
 954:     loadFlowContext();
 955:     updateExportControls();
 956: 
 957:     setTimeout(() => {
 958:       updateExportControls();
 959:     }, 500);
 960: 
 961:     setTimeout(() => {
 962:       updateExportControls();
 963:     }, 1200);
 964:   }
 965: 
 966:   bindEvents();
 967:   init();
 968: })();
